// app/(app)/layout.tsx
import React from "react";
import Navbar from "@/app/components/Navbar";
import Footer from "@/components/Footer";
import CommandPalette from "@/components/command-palette";
import WorkspaceSidebar from "@/components/layout/workspace-sidebar";

export const runtime = "nodejs";
export const dynamic = "force-dynamic";
export const revalidate = 0;

/**
 * IMPORTANT:
 * Do NOT enforce auth/org at the (app) layout level.
 * Layout-level redirects during RSC render cause "client-side exception"
 * + redirect loops.
 *
 * Enforce auth/org inside each protected page (or middleware), not here.
 */
export default function AppLayout({
  children,
}: {
  children: React.ReactNode;
}) {
  return (
    <div className="min-h-screen bg-gradient-to-b from-slate-950 via-slate-950 to-black text-white">
      <Navbar />

      <CommandPalette />

      <main id="main" className="min-h-[70vh]">
        <div className="mx-auto w-full max-w-[1560px] px-3 py-3 sm:px-4 lg:px-5">
          <div className="flex items-start gap-3 xl:gap-4">
            <div className="hidden xl:block xl:w-[268px] 2xl:w-[284px] shrink-0">
              <WorkspaceSidebar />
            </div>

            <div className="min-w-0 flex-1">
              {children}
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </main>

      <Footer />
    </div>
  );
}

import React from "react";
import Link from "next/link";

export const runtime = "nodejs";
export const dynamic = "force-dynamic";
export const revalidate = 0;

function NavChip({ href, label }: { href: string; label: string }) {
  return (
    <Link
      href={href}
      className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1.5 text-xs font-medium text-white/80 transition hover:border-cyan-400/30 hover:bg-cyan-400/10 hover:text-cyan-100"
    >
      {label}
    </Link>
  );
}

function SideLink({ href, label, sublabel }: { href: string; label: string; sublabel: string }) {
  return (
    <Link
      href={href}
      className="block rounded-[20px] border border-white/10 bg-white/[0.04] px-4 py-3 transition hover:border-cyan-400/25 hover:bg-cyan-400/[0.08]"
    >
      <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-white">{label}</div>
      <div className="mt-1 text-xs leading-5 text-white/55">{sublabel}</div>
    </Link>
  );
}

export default function TruvernOpsLayout({

                INTERNAL ONLY

FILE: app\(app)\truvern\ops\page.tsx
====================================================================================================
import Link from "next/link";
import prisma from "@/lib/prisma";
import { requireTruvernOperator } from "@/lib/truvern-ops-access";
import { buildTruvernSlaSnapshot, formatSlaRemaining } from "@/lib/truvern-ops-sla";
import TruvernOpsQueueClient from "./truvern-ops-queue.client";

export const runtime = "nodejs";
export const dynamic = "force-dynamic";
export const revalidate = 0;

function clsx(...parts: Array<string | false | null | undefined>) {
  return parts.filter(Boolean).join(" ");
}

function safeStr(v: unknown) {
  return typeof v === "string" ? v.trim() : "";
}

function upper(v: unknown) {
  return safeStr(v).toUpperCase();
}

function titleCase(v: unknown) {
  return safeStr(v)
    .toLowerCase()
    .split(/[\s_]+/)
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map((part) => part.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + part.slice(1))
    .join(" ");
}

function statusTone(status: string) {
  if (status === "IN_REVIEW") return "border-violet-400/30 bg-violet-400/12 text-violet-100";
  if (status === "COMPLETED") return "border-emerald-400/30 bg-emerald-400/12 text-emerald-100";
  if (status === "RELEASED") return "border-cyan-400/30 bg-cyan-400/12 text-cyan-100";
  if (status === "ASSIGNED") return "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-100";
  if (status === "AWAITING_ASSIGNMENT") {
    return "border-fuchsia-400/30 bg-fuchsia-400/12 text-fuchsia-100";
  }
  return "border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white/65";
}

function priorityTone(priority: string) {
  if (priority === "URGENT") return "border-rose-400/30 bg-rose-400/12 text-rose-100";
  if (priority === "HIGH") return "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-100";
  if (priority === "NORMAL") return "border-cyan-400/30 bg-cyan-400/12 text-cyan-100";
  if (priority === "LOW") return "border-emerald-400/30 bg-emerald-400/12 text-emerald-100";
  return "border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white/65";
}

function slaTone(state: string) {
  if (state === "overdue") return "border-rose-400/30 bg-rose-400/12 text-rose-100";
  if (state === "due_soon") return "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-100";
  if (state === "healthy") return "border-emerald-400/30 bg-emerald-400/12 text-emerald-100";
  return "border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white/65";
}

function formatDateTime(value: Date | null | undefined) {
  if (!value) return "—";
  const d = value instanceof Date ? value : new Date(value);
  if (Number.isNaN(d.getTime())) return "—";

  return new Intl.DateTimeFormat("en-US", {
    month: "short",
    day: "numeric",
    year: "numeric",
    hour: "numeric",
    minute: "2-digit",
  }).format(d);
}

function queueSortScore(row: {
  slaState: string;
  assignee: string;
  status: string;
  dueAt: Date | null;
  priority: string;
  updatedAt: Date | null;
}) {
  const priorityWeight =
    row.priority === "URGENT"
      ? 0
      : row.priority === "HIGH"
        ? 1
        : row.priority === "NORMAL"
          ? 2
          : row.priority === "LOW"
            ? 3
            : 4;

  const slaWeight =
    row.slaState === "overdue"
      ? 0
      : row.slaState === "due_soon"
        ? 1
        : row.slaState === "healthy"
          ? 2
          : 3;

  const assignmentWeight = row.assignee ? 1 : 0;

  const statusWeight =
    row.status === "COMPLETED"
      ? 0
      : row.status === "IN_REVIEW"
        ? 1
        : row.status === "ASSIGNED"
          ? 2
          : row.status === "AWAITING_ASSIGNMENT"
            ? 3
            : row.status === "RELEASED"
              ? 4
              : 5;

  const dueWeight = row.dueAt ? row.dueAt.getTime() : Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER;
  const updatedWeight = row.updatedAt ? -row.updatedAt.getTime() : 0;

  return [slaWeight, priorityWeight, assignmentWeight, statusWeight, dueWeight, updatedWeight];
}

type QueueRow = {
  id: number;
  org: string;
  vendor: string;
  vendorMateriality: string;
  runId: number;
  run: string;
  dueAt: string;
  dueAtRaw: Date | null;
  submittedAt: string;
  submittedAtRaw: Date | null;
  updatedAt: string;
  updatedAtRaw: Date | null;
  status: string;
  priority: string;
  assignee: string;
  isMine: boolean;
  slaState: string;
  slaLabel: string;
  canClaimAndStart: boolean;
  canStart: boolean;
  canComplete: boolean;
  canRelease: boolean;
  canReopen: boolean;
  openHref: string;
};

export default async function TruvernOpsPage() {
  const { userId } = await requireTruvernOperator();

  const assignments = await prisma.assessmentReviewAssignment.findMany({
    where: {
      assignmentType: "TRUVERN",
    },
    include: {
      organization: {
        select: {
          id: true,
          name: true,
          slug: true,
        },
      },
      vendor: {
        select: {
          id: true,
          name: true,
          materiality: true,
        },
      },
      assessmentRun: {
        select: {
          id: true,
          title: true,
          dueAt: true,
          submittedAt: true,
          updatedAt: true,
        },
      },
    },
    orderBy: [{ updatedAt: "desc" }, { id: "desc" }],
    take: 200,
  });

  const rows: QueueRow[] = assignments
    .map((a) => {
      const status = upper(a.status);
      const priority = upper(a.priority);
      const assignee = safeStr(a.assessorUserId);
      const isMine = assignee === userId;

      const sla = buildTruvernSlaSnapshot({
        serviceLevel: priority === "URGENT" ? "URGENT" : "STANDARD",
        anchorAt: a.startedAt ?? a.createdAt,
      });

      const dueAtRaw = a.assessmentRun?.dueAt ?? null;
      const submittedAtRaw = a.assessmentRun?.submittedAt ?? null;
      const updatedAtRaw = a.assessmentRun?.updatedAt ?? a.updatedAt ?? null;

      return {
        id: a.id,
        org: safeStr(a.organization?.name) || "Unknown org",
        vendor: safeStr(a.vendor?.name) || "Unknown vendor",
        vendorMateriality: safeStr(a.vendor?.materiality) || "—",
        runId: a.assessmentRun?.id ?? 0,
        run:
          safeStr(a.assessmentRun?.title) ||
          (a.assessmentRun?.id ? `Run #${a.assessmentRun.id}` : "Unknown run"),
        dueAt: formatDateTime(dueAtRaw),
        dueAtRaw,
        submittedAt: formatDateTime(submittedAtRaw),
        submittedAtRaw,
        updatedAt: formatDateTime(updatedAtRaw),
        updatedAtRaw,
        status,
        priority,
        assignee,
        isMine,
        slaState: safeStr((sla as any)?.state) || "unknown",
        slaLabel: formatSlaRemaining(sla),
        canClaimAndStart:
          !assignee &&
          (status === "AWAITING_ASSIGNMENT" || status === "ASSIGNED"),
        canStart: isMine && status === "ASSIGNED",
        canComplete: isMine && status === "IN_REVIEW",
        canRelease: isMine && status === "COMPLETED",
        canReopen: isMine && status === "RELEASED",
        openHref: `/truvern/ops/reviews/${a.id}`,
      };
    })
    .sort((a, b) => {
      const aa = queueSortScore({
        slaState: a.slaState,
        assignee: a.assignee,
        status: a.status,
        dueAt: a.dueAtRaw,
        priority: a.priority,
        updatedAt: a.updatedAtRaw,
      });

      const bb = queueSortScore({
        slaState: b.slaState,
        assignee: b.assignee,
        status: b.status,
        dueAt: b.dueAtRaw,
        priority: b.priority,
        updatedAt: b.updatedAtRaw,
      });

      for (let i = 0; i < aa.length; i += 1) {
        if (aa[i] < bb[i]) return -1;
        if (aa[i] > bb[i]) return 1;
      }
      return a.id - b.id;
    });

  const myQueue = rows.filter((r) => r.isMine && r.status !== "RELEASED");
  const unassigned = rows.filter((r) => !r.assignee);
  const dueSoon = rows.filter((r) => r.slaState === "due_soon");
  const overdue = rows.filter((r) => r.slaState === "overdue");
  const awaitingRelease = rows.filter((r) => r.status === "COMPLETED");
  const completedToday = rows.filter((r) => r.status === "RELEASED");

  const summaryCards = [
    {
      label: "Overdue",
      value: overdue.length,
      tone: "border-rose-400/30 bg-rose-400/12 text-rose-100",
    },
    {
      label: "Due Soon",
      value: dueSoon.length,
      tone: "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-100",
    },
    {
      label: "My Work",
      value: myQueue.length,
      tone: "border-cyan-400/30 bg-cyan-400/12 text-cyan-100",
    },
    {
      label: "Unassigned",
      value: unassigned.length,
      tone: "border-violet-400/30 bg-violet-400/12 text-violet-100",
    },
    {
      label: "Awaiting Release",
      value: awaitingRelease.length,
      tone: "border-emerald-400/30 bg-emerald-400/12 text-emerald-100",
    },
  ];

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top,rgba(34,211,238,0.10),transparent_28%),radial-gradient(circle_at_top_right,rgba(217,70,239,0.10),transparent_24%),linear-gradient(180deg,#060816_0%,#09101c_40%,#0a1220_100%)] px-6 py-6 text-white">
      <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl">
        <div className="rounded-[28px] border border-white/10 bg-white/[0.05] p-6 shadow-[0_0_0_1px_rgba(255,255,255,0.03),0_24px_70px_rgba(0,0,0,0.30)] backdrop-blur">
          <div className="flex flex-wrap items-start justify-between gap-4">
            <div>
              <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.28em] text-cyan-300/85">
                Truvern Internal
              </div>
              <h1 className="mt-2 text-3xl font-semibold text-white">
                Review Command Center
              </h1>
              <p className="mt-2 max-w-3xl text-sm leading-6 text-white/68">
                Fast triage queue for Truvern-managed reviews. Claim and start from the queue,
                prioritize overdue work first, and move directly into the operator workspace when
                deeper handling is needed.
              </p>
            </div>

            <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
              <Link
                href="/truvern/ops"
                className="inline-flex h-10 items-center justify-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-4 text-sm font-medium text-white/80 transition hover:bg-white/10"
              >
                Refresh queue
              </Link>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="mt-5 grid gap-3 sm:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-5">
            {summaryCards.map((card) => (
              <div
                key={card.label}
                className="rounded-[20px] border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-4"
              >
                <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-white/45">
                  {card.label}
                </div>
                <div className="mt-2 flex items-center justify-between">
                  <div className="text-2xl font-semibold text-white">{card.value}</div>
                  <div
                    className={clsx(
                      "rounded-full border px-2.5 py-1 text-xs font-medium",
                      card.tone,
                    )}
                  >
                    Live
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="mt-5 grid gap-4 xl:grid-cols-[1.08fr_0.92fr]">
          <section className="rounded-[26px] border border-white/10 bg-white/[0.05] p-5 shadow-[0_0_0_1px_rgba(255,255,255,0.03),0_22px_60px_rgba(0,0,0,0.26)] backdrop-blur">
            <div className="flex flex-wrap items-start justify-between gap-3">
              <div>
                <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.24em] text-white/45">
                  Queue strategy
                </div>
                <div className="mt-1 text-lg font-semibold text-white">
                  Operator-first flow
                </div>
                <div className="mt-1.5 text-sm leading-6 text-white/68">
                  Overdue and due-soon reviews float to the top. Unassigned work is kept ahead of
                  already-owned healthy work so operators can reduce queue risk quickly.
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                <div className="rounded-full border border-rose-400/30 bg-rose-400/12 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-rose-100">
                  Overdue first
                </div>
                <div className="rounded-full border border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-amber-100">
                  Due soon next
                </div>
                <div className="rounded-full border border-violet-400/30 bg-violet-400/12 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-violet-100">
                  Unassigned prioritized
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="mt-4 space-y-6">
              <TruvernOpsQueueClient
                title="🔥 Overdue"
                subtitle="Immediate attention required"
                rows={overdue}
              />
              <TruvernOpsQueueClient
                title="⏱ Due Soon"
                subtitle="Approaching SLA threshold"
                rows={dueSoon}
              />
              <TruvernOpsQueueClient
                title="👤 My Work"
                subtitle="Assigned to you"
                rows={myQueue}
              />
              <TruvernOpsQueueClient
                title="📥 Unassigned"
                subtitle="Available to claim and start"
                rows={unassigned}
              />
              <TruvernOpsQueueClient
                title="✅ Awaiting Release"
                subtitle="Completed reviews ready for final release"
                rows={awaitingRelease}
              />
            </div>
          </section>

          <aside className="space-y-4">
            <section className="rounded-[26px] border border-white/10 bg-white/[0.05] p-5 shadow-[0_0_0_1px_rgba(255,255,255,0.03),0_22px_60px_rgba(0,0,0,0.26)] backdrop-blur">
              <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.24em] text-cyan-300/80">
                Queue status
              </div>
              <div className="mt-2 text-lg font-semibold text-white">Current operating picture</div>

              <div className="mt-4 space-y-3">
                {rows.slice(0, 6).map((row) => (
                  <div
                    key={row.id}
                    className="rounded-[18px] border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-3.5"
                  >
                    <div className="flex items-start justify-between gap-3">
                      <div className="min-w-0">
                        <div className="truncate text-sm font-semibold text-white">
                          {row.vendor}
                        </div>
                        <div className="mt-1 text-xs text-white/55">
                          {row.org} · {row.run}
                        </div>
                      </div>

                      <div
                        className={clsx(
                          "rounded-full border px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium",
                          slaTone(row.slaState),
                        )}
                      >
                        {row.slaLabel}
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    <div className="mt-3 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                      <div
                        className={clsx(
                          "rounded-full border px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium",
                          statusTone(row.status),
                        )}
                      >
                        {titleCase(row.status)}
                      </div>
                      <div
                        className={clsx(
                          "rounded-full border px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium",
                          priorityTone(row.priority),
                        )}
                      >
                        {titleCase(row.priority || "Normal")}
                      </div>
                      <div className="rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] text-white/65">
                        {row.assignee ? (row.isMine ? "You" : "Assigned") : "Unassigned"}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))}

                {!rows.length ? (
                  <div className="rounded-[18px] border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-4 text-sm text-white/60">
                    No Truvern assignments found.
                  </div>
                ) : null}
              </div>
            </section>

            <section className="rounded-[26px] border border-white/10 bg-white/[0.05] p-5 shadow-[0_0_0_1px_rgba(255,255,255,0.03),0_22px_60px_rgba(0,0,0,0.26)] backdrop-blur">
              <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.24em] text-emerald-300/80">
                Operator guidance
              </div>
              <div className="mt-2 text-lg font-semibold text-white">Fast handling pattern</div>
              <div className="mt-3 space-y-2 text-sm leading-6 text-white/68">
                <p>Use Claim &amp; start on unassigned work to eliminate extra queue clicks.</p>
                <p>Complete from the queue once outcome drafting is done in the review workspace.</p>
                <p>Release-ready work stays visible in its own section so finalization does not get buried under active reviews.</p>
              </div>
            </section>

            <section className="rounded-[26px] border border-white/10 bg-white/[0.05] p-5 shadow-[0_0_0_1px_rgba(255,255,255,0.03),0_22px_60px_rgba(0,0,0,0.26)] backdrop-blur">
              <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.24em] text-violet-300/80">
                Queue counts
              </div>
              <div className="mt-4 grid gap-3 sm:grid-cols-2">
                <div className="rounded-[18px] border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-3.5">
                  <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">
                    Total rows
                  </div>
                  <div className="mt-2 text-xl font-semibold text-white">{rows.length}</div>
                </div>
                <div className="rounded-[18px] border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-3.5">
                  <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">
                    Released
                  </div>
                  <div className="mt-2 text-xl font-semibold text-white">
                    {completedToday.length}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </section>
          </aside>
        </div>
      </div>
    </main>
  );
}

  params: RouteParams | Promise<RouteParams>;
  searchParams?: SearchParams | Promise<SearchParams>;

};

function num(v: unknown) {
  const m = String(v ?? "").match(/\d+/);
  if (!m) return null;
  const n = Number(m[0]);
  return Number.isFinite(n) && n > 0 ? Math.floor(n) : null;
}

function upper(v: unknown) {
  return safeStr(v).toUpperCase();
}

function titleCase(value: unknown) {
  return safeStr(value)
    .toLowerCase()
    .split(/[\s_]+/)
    .filter(Boolean)
    .map((part) => part.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + part.slice(1))
    .join(" ");
}

function pickOne(v: string | string[] | undefined) {
  return Array.isArray(v) ? v[0] : v;
}

function boolish(v: string | string[] | undefined) {
  const s = upper(pickOne(v));
  return s === "1" || s === "TRUE" || s === "YES" || s === "OPEN";
}

function looksUnauthorized(err: any) {
  const code = String(err?.code || "");
  if (code === "UNAUTHORIZED") return true;
  const msg = String(err?.message || err || "").toLowerCase();
  return msg.includes("unauthorized") || msg.includes("forbidden");
}

function looksNoOrg(err: any) {
  const code = String(err?.code || "");
  if (
    code === "NO_ACTIVE_ORG" ||
    code === "ORG_REQUIRED" ||
    code === "NO_ORGANIZATION" ||
    code === "ORG_NOT_FOUND"
  ) {
    return true;
  }

  const msg = String(err?.message || err || "").toLowerCase();
  return (
    msg.includes("no active org") ||
    msg.includes("select org") ||
    msg.includes("no organization context") ||
    msg.includes("no organization") ||
    msg.includes("org required")
  );
}

function buildPath(
  base: string,
  params: Record<string, string | number | null | undefined>,
) {
  const sp = new URLSearchParams();
  for (const [k, v] of Object.entries(params)) {
    if (v == null) continue;
    const s = String(v).trim();
    if (!s) continue;
    sp.set(k, s);
  }
  const qs = sp.toString();
  return `${base}${qs ? `?${qs}` : ""}`;
}

function buildCurrentPath(runId: number, searchParams?: SearchParams) {
  return buildPath(`/review-desk/reviews/${runId}`, {
    releasePreview: boolish(searchParams?.releasePreview) ? 1 : undefined,
  });
}

function isActionableAssignmentStatus(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  return (
    s === "ASSIGNED" ||
    s === "IN_REVIEW" ||
    s === "COMPLETED" ||
    s === "RELEASED"
  );
}

function isLiveAssignmentStatus(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  return (
    s === "ASSIGNED" ||
    s === "IN_REVIEW" ||
    s === "COMPLETED" ||
    s === "RELEASED"
  );
}

function isDraftishRunStatus(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  return s === "DRAFT" || s === "IN_PROGRESS" || s === "OPEN";
}

function isSubmittedRunStatus(v: unknown) {
  return upper(v) === "SUBMITTED";
}

function isReviewRunStatus(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  return s === "REVIEW" || s === "IN_REVIEW";
}

function isCompletedRunStatus(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  return s === "COMPLETED" || s === "COMPLETE" || s === "SEALED";
}

function isReleasedOutcomeState(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  return (
    s === "RELEASED" ||
    s === "PUBLIC" ||
    s === "SHARED" ||
    s === "SHARED_WITH_REQUESTER"
  );
}

function isInternalOnlyOutcomeState(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  return s === "INTERNAL" || s === "INTERNAL_ONLY";
}

function isDraftOutcomeState(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  return s === "DRAFT" || s === "PENDING";
}

function isWorkingOutcomeState(v: unknown) {
  return isDraftOutcomeState(v) || isInternalOnlyOutcomeState(v);
}

function isPlainObject(v: unknown): v is Record<string, unknown> {
  return !!v && typeof v === "object" && !Array.isArray(v);
}

function clampScore(v: unknown): number | null {
  const n = typeof v === "number" ? v : Number(v);
  if (!Number.isFinite(n)) return null;
  return Math.max(0, Math.min(100, n));
}

function pickScorePreview(templateSnapshot: unknown): Record<string, unknown> | null {
  if (!isPlainObject(templateSnapshot)) return null;
  const sp = (templateSnapshot as any).scorePreview;
  return isPlainObject(sp) ? (sp as Record<string, unknown>) : null;
}

function pickSnapshotId(templateSnapshot: unknown): number | null {
  const sp = pickScorePreview(templateSnapshot);
  if (!sp) return null;
  return num(sp.snapshotId);
}

function pickSealedHash(templateSnapshot: unknown): string {
  const sp = pickScorePreview(templateSnapshot);
  if (!sp) return "";
  return safeStr(sp.sealedHash);
}

function pickSealedAt(templateSnapshot: unknown): string {
  const sp = pickScorePreview(templateSnapshot);
  if (!sp) return "";
  return safeStr(sp.sealedAt || sp.computedAt);
}

function pickOverallScore(templateSnapshot: unknown): number | null {
  const sp = pickScorePreview(templateSnapshot);
  if (sp) {
    const score = clampScore(sp.overall);
    if (score !== null) return score;
  }

  if (isPlainObject(templateSnapshot) && isPlainObject((templateSnapshot as any).scoring)) {
    return clampScore((templateSnapshot as any).scoring.overall);
  }

  return null;
}

function normalizedRunStatus(
  status: unknown,
  completedAt: unknown,
  templateSnapshot: unknown,
) {
  const sealed =
    !!pickSnapshotId(templateSnapshot) ||
    !!pickSealedHash(templateSnapshot) ||
    !!pickSealedAt(templateSnapshot);

  if (sealed || isCompletedRunStatus(status) || !!completedAt) return "COMPLETED";
  if (isReviewRunStatus(status)) return "REVIEW";
  if (isSubmittedRunStatus(status)) return "SUBMITTED";
  if (isDraftishRunStatus(status)) return "IN_PROGRESS";
  return upper(status) || "UNKNOWN";
}

function fmtDate(v?: Date | null) {
  if (!v) return "—";
  return new Intl.DateTimeFormat("en-US", {
    month: "short",
    day: "numeric",
    year: "numeric",
  }).format(v);
}

function fmtDateTime(v?: Date | null | string) {
  if (!v) return "—";
  const dt = v instanceof Date ? v : new Date(String(v));
  if (!Number.isFinite(dt.getTime())) return "—";
  return new Intl.DateTimeFormat("en-US", {
    month: "short",
    day: "numeric",
    year: "numeric",
    hour: "numeric",
    minute: "2-digit",
  }).format(dt);
}

function badgeClass(status: string) {
  const s = upper(status);
  if (s === "COMPLETED") return "border-emerald-400/30 bg-emerald-400/12 text-emerald-200";
  if (s === "IN_REVIEW") return "border-cyan-400/30 bg-cyan-400/12 text-cyan-200";
  if (s === "ASSIGNED") return "border-fuchsia-400/30 bg-fuchsia-400/12 text-fuchsia-200";
  if (s === "RELEASED" || s === "PENDING" || s === "AWAITING_ASSIGNMENT") {
    return "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-200";
  }
  if (s === "SUBMITTED") return "border-violet-400/30 bg-violet-400/12 text-violet-200";
  if (s === "REVIEW") return "border-sky-400/30 bg-sky-400/12 text-sky-200";
  if (s === "IN_PROGRESS") return "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-200";
  return "border-white/15 bg-white/8 text-white/80";
}

function priorityClass(priority: string) {
  const p = upper(priority);
  if (p === "URGENT") return "border-rose-400/30 bg-rose-400/12 text-rose-200";
  if (p === "HIGH") return "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-200";
  if (p === "NORMAL") return "border-cyan-400/30 bg-cyan-400/12 text-cyan-200";
  if (p === "LOW") return "border-emerald-400/30 bg-emerald-400/12 text-emerald-200";
  return "border-white/15 bg-white/8 text-white/80";
}

function roleClass(role: string) {
  const r = upper(role);
  if (r === "OWNER") return "border-emerald-400/30 bg-emerald-400/12 text-emerald-200";
  if (r === "ADMIN") return "border-cyan-400/30 bg-cyan-400/12 text-cyan-200";
  if (r === "ANALYST") return "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-200";
  return "border-white/15 bg-white/8 text-white/80";
}

function decisionClass(value: string) {
  const s = upper(value);
  if (s === "APPROVE" || s === "APPROVED" || s === "PASS") {
    return "border-emerald-400/30 bg-emerald-400/12 text-emerald-200";
  }
  if (
    s === "APPROVE_WITH_CONDITIONS" ||
    s === "APPROVED_WITH_NOTES" ||
    s === "CONDITIONAL"
  ) {
    return "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-200";
  }
  if (s === "ESCALATE") {
    return "border-fuchsia-400/30 bg-fuchsia-400/12 text-fuchsia-200";
  }
  if (s === "REJECT" || s === "REJECTED" || s === "FAIL" || s === "CHANGES_REQUIRED") {
    return "border-rose-400/30 bg-rose-400/12 text-rose-200";
  }
  if (s === "PENDING") {
    return "border-cyan-400/30 bg-cyan-400/12 text-cyan-200";
  }
  return "border-white/15 bg-white/8 text-white/80";
}

function riskClass(value: string) {
  const s = upper(value);
  if (s === "LOW" || s === "LOW RISK") {
    return "border-emerald-400/30 bg-emerald-400/12 text-emerald-200";
  }
  if (s === "MEDIUM" || s === "MODERATE RISK") {
    return "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-200";
  }
  if (s === "HIGH" || s === "ELEVATED RISK") {
    return "border-orange-400/30 bg-orange-400/12 text-orange-200";
  }
  if (s === "CRITICAL") {
    return "border-rose-400/30 bg-rose-400/12 text-rose-200";
  }
  return "border-white/15 bg-white/8 text-white/80";
}

function releaseStateClass(value: string) {
  const s = upper(value);
  if (isReleasedOutcomeState(s)) return "border-emerald-400/30 bg-emerald-400/12 text-emerald-200";
  if (isInternalOnlyOutcomeState(s)) return "border-cyan-400/30 bg-cyan-400/12 text-cyan-200";
  if (isDraftOutcomeState(s)) return "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-200";
  return "border-white/15 bg-white/8 text-white/80";
}
function assignmentTypeLabel(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  if (s === "TRUVERN") return "Truvern Expert Review";
  if (s === "INTERNAL") return "Internal Review";
  return s || "Review";
}

function workspaceChipLabel(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  if (s === "TRUVERN") return "Truvern Review Space";
  if (s === "INTERNAL") return "Internal Review Space";
  return "Review Workspace";
}

function workspaceIntro(
  v: unknown,
  opts?: {
    isCustomerTruvern?: boolean;
    truvernOpsReleased?: boolean;
    customerConfirmed?: boolean;
  },
) {
  const s = upper(v);
  const isCustomerTruvern = !!opts?.isCustomerTruvern;
  const truvernOpsReleased = !!opts?.truvernOpsReleased;
  const customerConfirmed = !!opts?.customerConfirmed;

  if (s === "TRUVERN" && isCustomerTruvern) {
    if (customerConfirmed) {
      return "This customer-facing Truvern review workspace now reflects the confirmed released baseline, including vendor context, lifecycle completion, and the final customer-visible recommendation.";
    }
    if (truvernOpsReleased) {
      return "Truvern has published the expert release. Review the final preview and confirm release to make this the official customer-facing baseline.";
    }
    return "This customer-facing Truvern review workspace shows lifecycle progression, vendor context, and release readiness. Until Truvern publishes and you confirm the expert release, working content remains hidden and only workflow progress is shown here.";
  }

  if (s === "TRUVERN") {
    return "This workspace gives Truvern reviewers the full context for the submitted package, canonical package assignment state, outcome record, stored scoring provenance, and audit trail for end-to-end review handling.";
  }

  if (s === "INTERNAL") {
    return "This workspace gives internal reviewers the full context for the submitted package, canonical package assignment state, outcome record, stored scoring provenance, and audit trail for end-to-end review handling.";
  }

  return "This workspace gives reviewers the full context for the submitted package, canonical package assignment state, outcome record, stored scoring provenance, and audit trail for end-to-end review handling.";
}

function outcomePanelTitle(
  v: unknown,
  opts?: {
    reopened?: boolean;
    hiddenForCustomer?: boolean;
    customerConfirmed?: boolean;
    truvernOpsReleased?: boolean;
  },
) {
  const s = upper(v);
  const reopened = !!opts?.reopened;
  const hiddenForCustomer = !!opts?.hiddenForCustomer;
  const customerConfirmed = !!opts?.customerConfirmed;
  const truvernOpsReleased = !!opts?.truvernOpsReleased;

  if (hiddenForCustomer && s === "TRUVERN") return "Truvern release-gated snapshot";
  if (customerConfirmed && s === "TRUVERN") return "Released Truvern review snapshot";
  if (truvernOpsReleased && s === "TRUVERN") return "Truvern released recommendation snapshot";
  if (reopened && s === "TRUVERN") return "Truvern working recommendation snapshot";
  if (reopened && s === "INTERNAL") return "Internal working review snapshot";
  if (reopened) return "Working review snapshot";
  if (s === "TRUVERN") return "Truvern recommendation snapshot";
  if (s === "INTERNAL") return "Internal review snapshot";
  return "Review snapshot";
}

function normalizeTimelineAction(action: unknown) {
  const a = upper(action);
  switch (a) {
    case "TRUVERN_REVIEW_PAYMENT_SIMULATED":
      return "Payment simulated";
    case "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_ASSIGNED_TRUVERN":
      return "Assigned to Truvern";
    case "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_ASSIGNED_INTERNAL":
      return "Assigned internally";
    case "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_RELEASED":
      return "Released";
    case "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_STARTED":
      return "Review started";
    case "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_IN_REVIEW":
      return "Moved to in review";
    case "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_COMPLETED":
      return "Review completed";
    case "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_FINDINGS_SAVED":
      return "Outcome version saved";
    default:
      return a || "Event";
  }
}

function summarizeAnswers(raw: unknown) {
  if (Array.isArray(raw)) return raw.length;
  if (raw && typeof raw === "object") return Object.keys(raw as Record<string, unknown>).length;
  return 0;
}

function renderJsonPreview(value: unknown) {
  try {
    return JSON.stringify(value, null, 2);
  } catch {
    return String(value ?? "");
  }
}

function pickMetaString(meta: unknown, key: string) {
  if (!meta || typeof meta !== "object") return "";
  return safeStr((meta as Record<string, unknown>)[key]);
}

function pickFindingsString(findings: unknown, key: string) {
  if (!findings || typeof findings !== "object") return "";
  return safeStr((findings as Record<string, unknown>)[key]);
}

function resolvePersonLabel(
  person:
    | {
        id?: number | null;
        userId?: string | null;
        role?: string | null;
        user?: {
          id?: number | null;
          name?: string | null;
          email?: string | null;
          displayName?: string | null;
          clerkUserId?: string | null;
        } | null;
      }
    | null
    | undefined,
  fallback = "Organization member",
) {
  const displayName = safeStr(person?.user?.displayName);
  const name = safeStr(person?.user?.name);
  const email = safeStr(person?.user?.email);
  const role = safeStr(person?.role);
  const membershipId =
    typeof person?.id === "number" && person.id > 0 ? String(person.id) : "";
  const clerkUserId = safeStr(person?.userId);

  if (displayName) return displayName;
  if (name) return name;
  if (email) return email;
  if (role && membershipId) return `${role} · member #${membershipId}`;
  if (role) return role;
  if (membershipId) return `${fallback} #${membershipId}`;
  if (clerkUserId) return fallback;

  return fallback;
}

function outcomeDisplayLabel(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  if (s === "APPROVED") return "APPROVE";
  if (s === "APPROVED_WITH_NOTES") return "APPROVE_WITH_CONDITIONS";
  if (s === "CHANGES_REQUIRED") return "REJECT";
  if (s === "REJECTED") return "ESCALATE";
  return s || "PENDING";
}

function prettyDecisionLabel(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  if (s === "APPROVE" || s === "APPROVED") return "Approve";
  if (s === "APPROVE_WITH_CONDITIONS" || s === "APPROVED_WITH_NOTES" || s === "CONDITIONAL") {
    return "Approve with Conditions";
  }
  if (s === "REJECT" || s === "CHANGES_REQUIRED" || s === "FAIL") return "Reject";
  if (s === "ESCALATE" || s === "REJECTED") return "Escalate";
  return "Pending";
}

function normalizeRiskLabel(v: unknown) {
  const s = upper(v);
  if (s === "LOW" || s === "LOW RISK") return "LOW";
  if (s === "MEDIUM" || s === "MODERATE" || s === "MODERATE RISK") return "MEDIUM";
  if (s === "HIGH" || s === "ELEVATED" || s === "ELEVATED RISK") return "HIGH";
  if (s === "CRITICAL") return "CRITICAL";
  return s || "MEDIUM";
}

function prettyRiskLabel(v: unknown) {
  const s = normalizeRiskLabel(v);
  if (s === "LOW") return "Low";
  if (s === "MEDIUM") return "Medium";
  if (s === "HIGH") return "High";
  if (s === "CRITICAL") return "Critical";
  return "Medium";
}

function decisionPillTone(value: unknown) {
  const s = upper(value);
  if (s === "APPROVE" || s === "APPROVED") return "border-emerald-400/30 bg-emerald-400/12 text-emerald-100";
  if (s === "APPROVE_WITH_CONDITIONS" || s === "APPROVED_WITH_NOTES" || s === "CONDITIONAL") {
    return "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-100";
  }
  if (s === "REJECT" || s === "CHANGES_REQUIRED" || s === "FAIL") {
    return "border-rose-400/30 bg-rose-400/12 text-rose-100";
  }
  if (s === "ESCALATE" || s === "REJECTED") {
    return "border-fuchsia-400/30 bg-fuchsia-400/12 text-fuchsia-100";
  }
  return "border-cyan-400/30 bg-cyan-400/12 text-cyan-100";
}

function riskPillTone(value: unknown) {
  const s = normalizeRiskLabel(value);
  if (s === "LOW") return "border-emerald-400/30 bg-emerald-400/12 text-emerald-100";
  if (s === "MEDIUM") return "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-100";
  if (s === "HIGH") return "border-orange-400/30 bg-orange-400/12 text-orange-100";
  if (s === "CRITICAL") return "border-rose-400/30 bg-rose-400/12 text-rose-100";
  return "border-white/15 bg-white/8 text-white/80";
}

function riskLabelFromScore(score: number | null) {
  if (score === null) return "—";
  if (score >= 85) return "Low risk";
  if (score >= 65) return "Moderate risk";
  if (score >= 40) return "Elevated risk";
  return "Critical";
}

function resolveOutcomeDecision(args: {
  outcome?: string | null;
  decision?: string | null;
  meta?: unknown;
  findings?: unknown;
}) {
  const raw =
    safeStr(args.decision) ||
    safeStr(args.outcome) ||
    pickMetaString(args.meta, "decision") ||
    pickMetaString(args.meta, "outcome") ||
    pickMetaString(args.meta, "recommendation") ||
    pickMetaString(args.meta, "decisionLabel") ||
    pickFindingsString(args.findings, "decision") ||
    pickFindingsString(args.findings, "outcome") ||
    pickFindingsString(args.findings, "recommendation") ||
    pickFindingsString(args.findings, "decisionLabel");

  return outcomeDisplayLabel(raw);
}

function resolveOutcomeRisk(args: {
  riskLevel?: string | null;
  meta?: unknown;
  findings?: unknown;
  templateSnapshot?: unknown;
}) {
  const raw =
    safeStr(args.riskLevel) ||
    pickMetaString(args.meta, "riskLevel") ||
    pickMetaString(args.meta, "residualRisk") ||
    pickFindingsString(args.findings, "riskLevel") ||
    pickFindingsString(args.findings, "residualRisk");

  if (raw) return raw;
  return riskLabelFromScore(pickOverallScore(args.templateSnapshot));
}

function nextActionForStatus(
  status: unknown,
): "start" | "complete" | "release" | "reopen" | null {
  const s = upper(status);
  if (s === "ASSIGNED") return "start";
  if (s === "IN_REVIEW") return "complete";
  if (s === "COMPLETED") return "release";
  if (s === "RELEASED") return "reopen";
  return null;
}

function progressionForStatus(
  status: unknown,
  packageCount: number,
  opts?: {
    reopened?: boolean;
    hasReleasedBaseline?: boolean;
    isCustomerTruvern?: boolean;
    truvernOpsReleased?: boolean;
    customerConfirmed?: boolean;
  },
) {
  const s = upper(status);
  const reopened = !!opts?.reopened;
  const hasReleasedBaseline = !!opts?.hasReleasedBaseline;
  const isCustomerTruvern = !!opts?.isCustomerTruvern;
  const truvernOpsReleased = !!opts?.truvernOpsReleased;
  const customerConfirmed = !!opts?.customerConfirmed;
  const packageSuffix =
    packageCount > 1 ? ` across ${packageCount} linked package assessments.` : ".";

  if (isCustomerTruvern && customerConfirmed) {
    return {
      currentStep: 4,
      heading: "Released customer baseline is active",
      body:
        "The Truvern expert release has already been confirmed by the customer. The released baseline is now active for this workspace.",
    };
  }

  if (isCustomerTruvern && truvernOpsReleased) {
    return {
      currentStep: 3,
      heading: "Customer confirm release is ready",
      body:
        "Truvern has published the expert release. Review the final preview and confirm release to make it the active customer-facing baseline.",
    };
  }

  if (isCustomerTruvern && !truvernOpsReleased) {
    return {
      currentStep: 3,
      heading: "Waiting for Truvern release",
      body:
        "Truvern has completed the expert review, but the expert release has not been published yet. Customer preview and confirm actions will unlock only after Truvern releases the review from the Truvern control center.",
    };
  }

  if (s === "ASSIGNED") {
    return {
      currentStep: 1,
      heading: reopened ? "Reopened review is queued to restart" : "Next step: start review",
      body: reopened
        ? "A previously released outcome exists, but a new review cycle has been opened. Starting review begins the next versioned cycle while preserving the last released result." +
          packageSuffix
        : "This assignment is ready to begin. Start review to move the workspace into active review handling" +
          packageSuffix,
    };
  }

  if (s === "IN_REVIEW") {
    return {
      currentStep: 2,
      heading: reopened ? "Reopened version is in progress" : "Next step: complete review",
      body: reopened
        ? "A prior released outcome remains preserved for downstream consumers while the reviewer works on a new draft version." +
          packageSuffix
        : "The review is actively being worked. Complete the review after the reviewer has finished analysis and findings are ready" +
          packageSuffix,
    };
  }

  if (s === "COMPLETED") {
    return {
      currentStep: 3,
      heading: reopened ? "Reopened version is ready to release" : "Next step: release review",
      body: reopened
        ? "The reopened review cycle is complete. Releasing now should publish the new version while superseding the previously released baseline downstream." +
          packageSuffix
        : "Review work is finished. Release review to finalize the lifecycle and mark the canonical package review as complete downstream" +
          packageSuffix,
    };
  }

  if (s === "RELEASED") {
    return {
      currentStep: 4,
      heading: hasReleasedBaseline ? "Released baseline is active" : "Lifecycle complete",
      body: hasReleasedBaseline
        ? "The latest released version is currently the active baseline."
        : "This review has already been released. No additional lifecycle action is available from this workspace.",
    };
  }

  return {
    currentStep: 0,
    heading: "Lifecycle unavailable",
    body: "No lifecycle progression is currently available for this review assignment.",
  };
}

function progressionStepTone(stepIndex: number, currentStep: number) {
  if (currentStep >= 4 && stepIndex <= 4) {
    return "border-emerald-400/25 bg-emerald-400/10 text-emerald-100";
  }
  if (stepIndex < currentStep) {
    return "border-emerald-400/25 bg-emerald-400/10 text-emerald-100";
  }
  if (stepIndex === currentStep) {
    return "border-cyan-400/30 bg-cyan-400/12 text-cyan-100";
  }
  return "border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white/55";
}

function actionLabel(
  action: "start" | "complete" | "release" | "reopen" | null,
  packageCount: number,
  opts?: {
    reviewStatus?: string;
    hasReleasedBaseline?: boolean;
    isCustomerTruvern?: boolean;
    customerPreviewEnabled?: boolean;
    customerConfirmed?: boolean;
  },
) {
  const status = upper(opts?.reviewStatus);
  const hasReleasedBaseline = !!opts?.hasReleasedBaseline;
  const isCustomerTruvern = !!opts?.isCustomerTruvern;
  const customerPreviewEnabled = !!opts?.customerPreviewEnabled;
  const customerConfirmed = !!opts?.customerConfirmed;

  if (isCustomerTruvern && customerConfirmed) return "None";
  if (isCustomerTruvern && customerPreviewEnabled) {
    return "Review release preview → Confirm release";
  }
  if (isCustomerTruvern && !customerPreviewEnabled) {
    return "Waiting for Truvern release";
  }
  if (status === "RELEASED" && hasReleasedBaseline) {
    return packageCount > 1 ? "Reopen package review" : "Reopen review";
  }
  if (action === "reopen") return packageCount > 1 ? "Reopen package review" : "Reopen review";
  if (action === "start") return packageCount > 1 ? "Start package review" : "Start review";
  if (action === "complete") return packageCount > 1 ? "Complete package review" : "Complete review";
  if (action === "release") return packageCount > 1 ? "Release package review" : "Release review";
  return "None";
}

function latestTs(...values: Array<Date | null | undefined>) {
  let best: Date | null = null;
  for (const value of values) {
    if (!value) continue;
    if (!best || value.getTime() > best.getTime()) best = value;
  }
  return best;
}

function earliestTs(...values: Array<Date | null | undefined>) {
  let best: Date | null = null;
  for (const value of values) {
    if (!value) continue;
    if (!best || value.getTime() < best.getTime()) best = value;
  }
  return best;
}

function avgScore(values: Array<number | null | undefined>) {
  const valid = values.filter((v): v is number => typeof v === "number" && Number.isFinite(v));
  if (!valid.length) return null;
  return Math.round(valid.reduce((sum, v) => sum + v, 0) / valid.length);
}

function packageReviewLabel(count: number) {
  return count === 1 ? "Single assessment submission" : `Submitted package · ${count} assessments`;
}

function packageReleaseSummary(values: string[]) {
  const normalized = values.map((v) => upper(v)).filter(Boolean);
  if (!normalized.length) return "No saved outcomes";
  const releasedCount = normalized.filter((v) => isReleasedOutcomeState(v)).length;
  const internalCount = normalized.filter((v) => isInternalOnlyOutcomeState(v)).length;
  const draftCount = normalized.filter((v) => isDraftOutcomeState(v)).length;

  if (releasedCount === normalized.length) return "Fully released";
  if (releasedCount > 0) return `Partially released · ${releasedCount}/${normalized.length}`;
  if (internalCount === normalized.length) return "Internal only";
  if (draftCount === normalized.length) return "Draft only";
  return "Mixed release states";
}

function packageDecisionSummary(values: string[]) {
  const normalized = values.map((v) => upper(v)).filter(Boolean);
  if (!normalized.length) return "No saved decisions";
  const counts = new Map<string, number>();
  for (const value of normalized) counts.set(value, (counts.get(value) ?? 0) + 1);
  const sorted = [...counts.entries()].sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1]);
  const [topLabel, topCount] = sorted[0];
  if (sorted.length === 1) return `${topLabel} across package`;
  return `${topLabel} leads · ${topCount}/${normalized.length}`;
}

function packageRiskSummary(values: string[]) {
  const normalized = values.map((v) => upper(v)).filter(Boolean);
  if (!normalized.length) return "No saved risk bands";
  if (normalized.includes("CRITICAL")) return "Contains critical residual risk";
  if (normalized.includes("HIGH") || normalized.includes("ELEVATED RISK")) {
    return "Contains elevated residual risk";
  }
  if (normalized.includes("MEDIUM") || normalized.includes("MODERATE RISK")) {
    return "Moderate residual risk across package";
  }
  if (normalized.every((v) => v === "LOW" || v === "LOW RISK")) {
    return "Low residual risk across package";
  }
  return "Mixed residual risk";
}

function packageRunStatusLabel(
  statuses: string[],
  releaseStates: string[],
  assignmentStatuses: string[],
) {
  const normalizedStatuses = statuses.map((s) => upper(s)).filter(Boolean);
  const normalizedReleases = releaseStates.map((s) => upper(s)).filter(Boolean);
  const normalizedAssignments = assignmentStatuses.map((s) => upper(s)).filter(Boolean);

  if (normalizedReleases.length > 0 && normalizedReleases.every((s) => isReleasedOutcomeState(s))) {
    return "RELEASED";
  }
  if (normalizedAssignments.some((s) => s === "COMPLETED")) return "COMPLETED";
  if (normalizedAssignments.some((s) => s === "IN_REVIEW")) return "IN_REVIEW";
  if (normalizedAssignments.some((s) => s === "ASSIGNED")) return "ASSIGNED";
  if (normalizedStatuses.length > 0 && normalizedStatuses.every((s) => s === "COMPLETED")) {
    return "COMPLETED";
  }
  if (normalizedStatuses.some((s) => s === "REVIEW")) return "REVIEW";
  if (normalizedStatuses.some((s) => s === "SUBMITTED")) return "SUBMITTED";
  if (normalizedStatuses.some((s) => s === "IN_PROGRESS")) return "IN_PROGRESS";
  return normalizedStatuses[0] || "UNKNOWN";
}

function choosePackagePrimaryRun<
  T extends { id: number; dueAt?: Date | null; submittedAt?: Date | null; createdAt?: Date | null },
>(runs: T[]) {
  if (!runs.length) return null;
  return [...runs].sort((a, b) => {
    const dueA = a.dueAt ? new Date(a.dueAt).getTime() : Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER;
    const dueB = b.dueAt ? new Date(b.dueAt).getTime() : Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER;
    if (dueA !== dueB) return dueA - dueB;

    const submittedA = a.submittedAt ? new Date(a.submittedAt).getTime() : Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER;
    const submittedB = b.submittedAt ? new Date(b.submittedAt).getTime() : Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER;
    if (submittedA !== submittedB) return submittedA - submittedB;

    const createdA = a.createdAt ? new Date(a.createdAt).getTime() : Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER;
    const createdB = b.createdAt ? new Date(b.createdAt).getTime() : Number.MAX_SAFE_INTEGER;
    if (createdA !== createdB) return createdA - createdB;

    return a.id - b.id;
  })[0];
}

function canActorOpenAssignedWorkspace(args: {
  actorUserId: string;
  actorRole: string;
  assignment:
    | {
        assignmentType?: string | null;
        status?: string | null;
        assessorUserId?: string | null;
        membership?: { userId?: string | null } | null;
      }
    | null
    | undefined;
}) {
  const assignmentType = upper(args.assignment?.assignmentType);
  const latestStatus = safeStr(args.assignment?.status).toUpperCase();
  const isLiveAssignedWorkspace =
    latestStatus === "ASSIGNED" ||
    latestStatus === "IN_REVIEW" ||
    latestStatus === "COMPLETED" ||
    latestStatus === "RELEASED";

  if (assignmentType === "TRUVERN" && isLiveAssignedWorkspace) return true;
  if (isInternalAssessorRole(args.actorRole)) return true;

  const assignedUserId =
    safeStr(args.assignment?.assessorUserId) ||
    safeStr(args.assignment?.membership?.userId) ||
    "";

  return !!assignedUserId && assignedUserId === safeStr(args.actorUserId) && isLiveAssignedWorkspace;
}

function normalizePreviewText(value: string) {
  return safeStr(value) || "—";
}

function buildReleaseDiffItems(args: {
  releasedExecutiveSummary: string;
  draftExecutiveSummary: string;
  releasedFindings: string;
  draftFindings: string;
  releasedRemediation: string;
  draftRemediation: string;
  releasedDecision: string;
  draftDecision: string;
  releasedRisk: string;
  draftRisk: string;
}): DiffItem[] {
  return [
    {
      label: "Executive summary",
      released: normalizePreviewText(args.releasedExecutiveSummary),
      draft: normalizePreviewText(args.draftExecutiveSummary),
      changed:
        normalizePreviewText(args.releasedExecutiveSummary) !==
        normalizePreviewText(args.draftExecutiveSummary),
    },
    {
      label: "Decision",
      released: normalizePreviewText(args.releasedDecision),
      draft: normalizePreviewText(args.draftDecision),
      changed:
        normalizePreviewText(args.releasedDecision) !==
        normalizePreviewText(args.draftDecision),
    },
    {
      label: "Residual risk",
      released: normalizePreviewText(args.releasedRisk),
      draft: normalizePreviewText(args.draftRisk),
      changed:
        normalizePreviewText(args.releasedRisk) !==
        normalizePreviewText(args.draftRisk),
    },
    {
      label: "Key findings",
      released: normalizePreviewText(args.releasedFindings),
      draft: normalizePreviewText(args.draftFindings),
      changed:
        normalizePreviewText(args.releasedFindings) !==
        normalizePreviewText(args.draftFindings),
    },
    {
      label: "Remediation / follow-up",
      released: normalizePreviewText(args.releasedRemediation),
      draft: normalizePreviewText(args.draftRemediation),
      changed:
        normalizePreviewText(args.releasedRemediation) !==
        normalizePreviewText(args.draftRemediation),
    },
  ];
}

function diffPillTone(label: string, value: string) {
  const key = upper(label);
  if (key === "DECISION") return decisionPillTone(value);
  if (key === "RESIDUAL RISK") return riskPillTone(value);
  return "border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white/75";
}

function diffDisplayValue(label: string, value: string) {
  const key = upper(label);
  if (key === "DECISION") return prettyDecisionLabel(value);
  if (key === "RESIDUAL RISK") return prettyRiskLabel(value);
  return value;
}

export default async function ReviewDeskReviewPage({ params, searchParams }: Props) {
  const p = (params ? await params : {}) as RouteParams;
  const resolvedSearchParams = ((searchParams ? await searchParams : {}) ?? {}) as SearchParams;

  const requestedRunId = num(p.id);
  if (!requestedRunId) notFound();

  const currentPath = buildCurrentPath(requestedRunId, resolvedSearchParams);

  let org: any;
  try {
    org = await requireDbOrganization();
  } catch (e: any) {
    if (looksUnauthorized(e)) {
      redirect(`/sign-in?redirect_url=${encodeURIComponent(currentPath)}`);
    }
    if (looksNoOrg(e)) {
      redirect(`/onboarding?redirect_url=${encodeURIComponent(currentPath)}`);
    }
    throw e;
  }

  let clerkUserId = "";
  try {
    const a = await auth();
    clerkUserId = safeStr(a?.userId);
  } catch {
    clerkUserId = "";
  }

  if (!clerkUserId) {
    return <ReviewDeskNotAuthorized />;
  }

  const [actorMembership, creditSummary] = await Promise.all([
    prisma.orgMembership.findFirst({
      where: { organizationId: org.id, userId: clerkUserId },
      select: { id: true, role: true },
    }),
    getTruvernCreditSummary(org.id),
  ]);

  const actorRole = normalizeOrgRole(actorMembership?.role);

  if (!actorMembership || !isReviewDeskRole(actorRole)) {
    return <ReviewDeskNotAuthorized />;
  }

  const availableCredits = Number(creditSummary?.balance?.available ?? 0);
  const reservedCredits = Number(creditSummary?.balance?.reserved ?? 0);
  const consumedCredits = Number(creditSummary?.balance?.consumed ?? 0);
  const minimumBalanceAlert =
    typeof creditSummary?.policy?.minimumBalanceAlert === "number"
      ? creditSummary.policy.minimumBalanceAlert
      : null;

  const requestedRun = (await prisma.assessmentRun.findFirst({
    where: { id: requestedRunId, organizationId: org.id },
    select: {
      id: true,
      title: true,
      description: true,
      status: true,
      dueAt: true,
      submittedAt: true,
      createdAt: true,
      updatedAt: true,
      completedAt: true,
      answers: true,
      templateSnapshot: true,
      vendorId: true,
      vendor: {
        select: {
          id: true,
          name: true,
          criticality: true,
          materiality: true,
          contactName: true,
          contactEmail: true,
        },
      },
      template: {
        select: {
          id: true,
          name: true,
          description: true,
          standard: true,
          version: true,
          category: true,
        },
      },
      reviewAssignments: {
        orderBy: [{ createdAt: "desc" }],
        take: 20,
        select: {
          id: true,
          assignmentType: true,
          status: true,
          priority: true,
          note: true,
          advisoryAck: true,
          advisoryAckAt: true,
          assessorUserId: true,
          createdAt: true,
          updatedAt: true,
          startedAt: true,
          completedAt: true,
          membership: {
            select: {
              id: true,
              userId: true,
              role: true,
              user: {
                select: {
                  id: true,
                  name: true,
                  email: true,
                  displayName: true,
                  clerkUserId: true,
                },
              },
            },
          },
          requestedByMembership: {
            select: {
              id: true,
              userId: true,
              role: true,
              user: {
                select: {
                  id: true,
                  name: true,
                  email: true,
                  displayName: true,
                },
              },
            },
          },
        },
      },
    },
  })) as ReviewDeskRunRow | null;

  if (!requestedRun) notFound();

  const packageRuns: ReviewDeskRunRow[] =
    requestedRun.vendorId && requestedRun.submittedAt
      ? ((await prisma.assessmentRun.findMany({
          where: {
            organizationId: org.id,
            vendorId: requestedRun.vendorId,
            submittedAt: requestedRun.submittedAt,
          },
          orderBy: [{ updatedAt: "desc" }, { id: "desc" }],
          select: {
            id: true,
            title: true,
            description: true,
            status: true,
            dueAt: true,
            submittedAt: true,
            createdAt: true,
            updatedAt: true,
            completedAt: true,
            answers: true,
            templateSnapshot: true,
            vendorId: true,
            vendor: {
              select: {
                id: true,
                name: true,
                criticality: true,
                materiality: true,
                contactName: true,
                contactEmail: true,
              },
            },
            template: {
              select: {
                id: true,
                name: true,
                description: true,
                standard: true,
                version: true,
                category: true,
              },
            },
            reviewAssignments: {
              orderBy: [{ createdAt: "desc" }],
              take: 20,
              select: {
                id: true,
                assignmentType: true,
                status: true,
                priority: true,
                note: true,
                advisoryAck: true,
                advisoryAckAt: true,
                assessorUserId: true,
                createdAt: true,
                updatedAt: true,
                startedAt: true,
                completedAt: true,
                membership: {
                  select: {
                    id: true,
                    userId: true,
                    role: true,
                    user: {
                      select: {
                        id: true,
                        name: true,
                        email: true,
                        displayName: true,
                        clerkUserId: true,
                      },
                    },
                  },
                },
                requestedByMembership: {
                  select: {
                    id: true,
                    userId: true,
                    role: true,
                    user: {
                      select: {
                        id: true,
                        name: true,
                        email: true,
                        displayName: true,
                      },
                    },
                  },
                },
              },
            },
          },
        })) as ReviewDeskRunRow[])
      : [requestedRun];

  const primaryRun = choosePackagePrimaryRun(packageRuns) ?? requestedRun;
  const packageRunIds = packageRuns.map((r) => r.id);

  if (requestedRun.id !== primaryRun.id && packageRuns.length > 1) {
    redirect(`/review-desk/reviews/${primaryRun.id}`);
  }
  const [primaryTimeline, latestFindingsEvent, packageTimeline, packageOutcomesForTimeline, primaryOutcomes] =
    (await Promise.all([
      prisma.auditLog.findMany({
        where: {
          organizationId: org.id,
          entityType: "AssessmentRun",
          entityId: primaryRun.id,
          action: {
            in: [
              "TRUVERN_REVIEW_PAYMENT_SIMULATED",
              "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_ASSIGNED_TRUVERN",
              "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_ASSIGNED_INTERNAL",
              "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_RELEASED",
              "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_STARTED",
              "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_IN_REVIEW",
              "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_COMPLETED",
              ],
          },
        },
        orderBy: [{ createdAt: "desc" }, { id: "desc" }],
        take: 20,
        select: {
          id: true,
          entityId: true,
          action: true,
          summary: true,
          createdAt: true,
          meta: true,
          ip: true,
          actorMembershipId: true,
          actorUserId: true,
        },
      }),
      prisma.auditLog.findFirst({
        where: {
          organizationId: org.id,
          entityType: "AssessmentRun",
          entityId: primaryRun.id,
          action: "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_FINDINGS_SAVED",
        },
        orderBy: [{ createdAt: "desc" }, { id: "desc" }],
        select: {
          id: true,
          createdAt: true,
          summary: true,
          meta: true,
        },
      }),
      packageRunIds.length
        ? prisma.auditLog.findMany({
            where: {
              organizationId: org.id,
              entityType: "AssessmentRun",
              entityId: { in: packageRunIds },
              action: {
                in: [
                  "TRUVERN_REVIEW_PAYMENT_SIMULATED",
                  "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_ASSIGNED_TRUVERN",
                  "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_ASSIGNED_INTERNAL",
                  "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_RELEASED",
                  "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_STARTED",
                  "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_IN_REVIEW",
                  "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_COMPLETED",
                  ],
              },
            },
            orderBy: [{ createdAt: "desc" }, { id: "desc" }],
            take: 80,
            select: {
              id: true,
              entityId: true,
              action: true,
              summary: true,
              createdAt: true,
              meta: true,
              ip: true,
              actorMembershipId: true,
              actorUserId: true,
            },
          })
        : Promise.resolve([]),
      packageRunIds.length
        ? prisma.assessmentReviewOutcome.findMany({
            where: {
              organizationId: org.id,
              assessmentRunId: { in: packageRunIds },
              supersededAt: null,
            },
            orderBy: [{ submittedAt: "desc" }, { createdAt: "desc" }, { id: "desc" }],
            select: {
              id: true,
              assessmentRunId: true,
              assignmentId: true,
              assignmentType: true,
              outcome: true,
              decision: true,
              riskLevel: true,
              releaseState: true,
              summary: true,
              executiveSummary: true,
              note: true,
              reviewerNote: true,
              findings: true,
              findingsText: true,
              remediation: true,
              meta: true,
              submittedAt: true,
              releasedAt: true,
              supersededAt: true,
              createdAt: true,
              updatedAt: true,
            },
          })
        : Promise.resolve([]),
      prisma.assessmentReviewOutcome.findMany({
        where: {
          organizationId: org.id,
          assessmentRunId: primaryRun.id,
          supersededAt: null,
        },
        orderBy: [{ updatedAt: "desc" }, { createdAt: "desc" }, { id: "desc" }],
        select: {
          id: true,
          assessmentRunId: true,
          assignmentId: true,
          assignmentType: true,
          outcome: true,
          decision: true,
          riskLevel: true,
          releaseState: true,
          summary: true,
          executiveSummary: true,
          note: true,
          reviewerNote: true,
          findings: true,
          findingsText: true,
          remediation: true,
          meta: true,
          submittedAt: true,
          releasedAt: true,
          supersededAt: true,
          createdAt: true,
          updatedAt: true,
        },
      }),
    ])) as [
      ReviewDeskAuditLogRow[],
      {
        id: number;
        createdAt: Date;
        summary: string | null;
        meta: unknown;
      } | null,
      ReviewDeskAuditLogRow[],
      ReviewDeskOutcomeRow[],
      ReviewDeskOutcomeRow[],
    ];

  const latestCanonicalOutcome = primaryOutcomes[0] ?? null;
  const latestReleasedOutcome =
    primaryOutcomes.find((o) => isReleasedOutcomeState(o.releaseState)) ?? null;
  const latestWorkingOutcome =
    primaryOutcomes.find((o) => isWorkingOutcomeState(o.releaseState)) ?? null;

  const actionableAssignment =
    primaryRun.reviewAssignments.find((a) => isActionableAssignmentStatus(a.status)) ?? null;
  const latestAssignment = primaryRun.reviewAssignments[0] ?? null;
  const displayAssignment = actionableAssignment ?? latestAssignment ?? null;

  const effectiveAssignmentType =
    upper(
      displayAssignment?.assignmentType ||
        latestCanonicalOutcome?.assignmentType ||
        latestReleasedOutcome?.assignmentType,
    ) || "";

  const isTruvernWorkspace = effectiveAssignmentType === "TRUVERN";
  const isCustomerTruvernWorkspace = isTruvernWorkspace && !isInternalAssessorRole(actorRole);
  const hasReleasedBaseline = !!latestReleasedOutcome?.id;

  const actorCanOpenWorkspace = canActorOpenAssignedWorkspace({
    actorUserId: clerkUserId,
    actorRole,
    assignment: displayAssignment,
  });

  if (!actorCanOpenWorkspace) {
    return <ReviewDeskNotAuthorized />;
  }

  const latestReleasedMeta = latestReleasedOutcome?.meta ?? null;
  const latestCanonicalMeta = latestCanonicalOutcome?.meta ?? null;

  const assignmentLifecycleStatus = safeStr(displayAssignment?.status);
  const assignmentLifecycleStatusUpper = upper(assignmentLifecycleStatus);

  const truvernReleasedAt =
    pickMetaString(latestReleasedMeta, "truvernReleasedAt") ||
    pickMetaString(latestCanonicalMeta, "truvernReleasedAt") ||
    safeStr(latestReleasedOutcome?.releasedAt);

  const customerConfirmedAt =
    pickMetaString(latestReleasedMeta, "customerConfirmedAt") ||
    pickMetaString(latestCanonicalMeta, "customerConfirmedAt");

  const truvernOpsReleased =
    isCustomerTruvernWorkspace && (!!truvernReleasedAt || hasReleasedBaseline);

  const truvernCustomerAlreadyConfirmed =
    isCustomerTruvernWorkspace &&
    (!!customerConfirmedAt || assignmentLifecycleStatusUpper === "RELEASED");

  const truvernCustomerConfirmReady =
    isCustomerTruvernWorkspace &&
    truvernOpsReleased &&
    !truvernCustomerAlreadyConfirmed;

  const customerLifecycleStatus = isCustomerTruvernWorkspace
    ? truvernCustomerAlreadyConfirmed
      ? "RELEASED"
      : truvernCustomerConfirmReady
        ? "COMPLETED"
        : assignmentLifecycleStatus || "ASSIGNED"
    : assignmentLifecycleStatus ||
      (isReleasedOutcomeState(latestCanonicalOutcome?.releaseState) ? "RELEASED" : "") ||
      "";

  const truvernCustomerCanSeeContents =
    !isCustomerTruvernWorkspace || truvernCustomerAlreadyConfirmed;

  const shouldHideTruvernContents =
    isCustomerTruvernWorkspace && !truvernCustomerCanSeeContents;

  const visibleOutcome = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? null
    : latestReleasedOutcome ?? latestCanonicalOutcome;

  const canonicalOutcome = latestCanonicalOutcome ?? latestReleasedOutcome ?? null;
  const findingsSourceOutcome = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? null
    : visibleOutcome ?? canonicalOutcome;
  const findingsSourceMeta = findingsSourceOutcome?.meta ?? null;
  const findingsSourceJson = findingsSourceOutcome?.findings ?? null;

  const findingsExecutiveSummary = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? ""
    : safeStr(findingsSourceOutcome?.executiveSummary) ||
      safeStr(findingsSourceOutcome?.summary) ||
      pickMetaString(findingsSourceMeta, "executiveSummary") ||
      pickFindingsString(findingsSourceJson, "executiveSummary") ||
      pickFindingsString(findingsSourceJson, "boardSummary") ||
      "";

  const findingsDecision = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? "PENDING"
    : resolveOutcomeDecision({
        decision: findingsSourceOutcome?.decision ?? null,
        outcome: findingsSourceOutcome?.outcome ?? null,
        meta: findingsSourceMeta,
        findings: findingsSourceJson,
      }) ||
      pickMetaString(latestFindingsEvent?.meta, "decision") ||
      "PENDING";

  const findingsRiskLevel = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? "—"
    : resolveOutcomeRisk({
        riskLevel: findingsSourceOutcome?.riskLevel ?? null,
        meta: findingsSourceMeta,
        findings: findingsSourceJson,
        templateSnapshot: primaryRun.templateSnapshot,
      }) || pickMetaString(latestFindingsEvent?.meta, "riskLevel");

  const findingsText = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? ""
    : safeStr(findingsSourceOutcome?.findingsText) ||
      pickMetaString(findingsSourceMeta, "findings") ||
      pickFindingsString(findingsSourceJson, "findings") ||
      pickMetaString(latestFindingsEvent?.meta, "findings");

  const findingsRemediation = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? ""
    : safeStr(findingsSourceOutcome?.remediation) ||
      pickMetaString(findingsSourceMeta, "remediation") ||
      pickFindingsString(findingsSourceJson, "remediation") ||
      pickMetaString(latestFindingsEvent?.meta, "remediation");

  const findingsReviewerNote = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? ""
    : safeStr(findingsSourceOutcome?.reviewerNote) ||
      safeStr(findingsSourceOutcome?.note) ||
      pickMetaString(findingsSourceMeta, "reviewerNote") ||
      pickFindingsString(findingsSourceJson, "reviewerNote") ||
      pickMetaString(latestFindingsEvent?.meta, "reviewerNote");

  const canonicalSavedAt = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? null
    : canonicalOutcome?.updatedAt ??
      canonicalOutcome?.submittedAt ??
      latestReleasedOutcome?.updatedAt ??
      latestReleasedOutcome?.submittedAt ??
      null;

  const lastFindingsSavedAt = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? ""
    : canonicalSavedAt
      ? fmtDateTime(canonicalSavedAt)
      : latestFindingsEvent?.createdAt
        ? fmtDateTime(latestFindingsEvent.createdAt)
        : "";

  const canonicalAssignmentId =
    typeof visibleOutcome?.assignmentId === "number" && visibleOutcome.assignmentId > 0
      ? visibleOutcome.assignmentId
      : typeof displayAssignment?.id === "number" && displayAssignment.id > 0
        ? displayAssignment.id
        : null;

  const normalizedStatus = normalizedRunStatus(
    primaryRun.status,
    primaryRun.completedAt,
    primaryRun.templateSnapshot,
  );

  const overallScore = pickOverallScore(primaryRun.templateSnapshot);
  const snapshotId = pickSnapshotId(primaryRun.templateSnapshot);
  const sealedHash = pickSealedHash(primaryRun.templateSnapshot);
  const sealedAt = pickSealedAt(primaryRun.templateSnapshot);
  const answersCount =
    summarizeAnswers(primaryRun.answers) ||
    summarizeAnswers(
      isPlainObject(primaryRun.templateSnapshot)
        ? primaryRun.templateSnapshot["answers"]
        : null,
    );

  const laneLabel = assignmentTypeLabel(effectiveAssignmentType);
  const workspaceLabel = workspaceChipLabel(effectiveAssignmentType);
  const workspaceBody = workspaceIntro(effectiveAssignmentType, {
    isCustomerTruvern: isCustomerTruvernWorkspace,
    truvernOpsReleased,
    customerConfirmed: truvernCustomerAlreadyConfirmed,
  });

  const isReopenedReview =
    !!displayAssignment &&
    isLiveAssignmentStatus(displayAssignment.status) &&
    hasReleasedBaseline &&
    upper(displayAssignment.status) !== "RELEASED" &&
    !isCustomerTruvernWorkspace;

  const snapshotTitle = outcomePanelTitle(effectiveAssignmentType, {
    reopened: isReopenedReview,
    hiddenForCustomer: shouldHideTruvernContents,
    customerConfirmed: truvernCustomerAlreadyConfirmed,
    truvernOpsReleased,
  });

  const requestorName = resolvePersonLabel(
    displayAssignment?.requestedByMembership,
    upper(displayAssignment?.assignmentType) === "TRUVERN"
      ? "Truvern request"
      : "Organization member",
  );

  const assignedName =
    safeStr(displayAssignment?.membership?.user?.displayName) ||
    safeStr(displayAssignment?.membership?.user?.name) ||
    safeStr(displayAssignment?.membership?.user?.email) ||
    (upper(displayAssignment?.assignmentType) === "TRUVERN"
      ? "Truvern Analyst Team"
      : "Unassigned");

  const progression = progressionForStatus(customerLifecycleStatus, packageRuns.length, {
    reopened: isReopenedReview,
    hasReleasedBaseline,
    isCustomerTruvern: isCustomerTruvernWorkspace,
    truvernOpsReleased,
    customerConfirmed: truvernCustomerAlreadyConfirmed,
  });

  const nextAction = nextActionForStatus(customerLifecycleStatus);

  const packageSummaries = packageRuns
    .map((pkgRun) => {
      const pkgActionableAssignment =
        pkgRun.reviewAssignments.find((a) => isActionableAssignmentStatus(a.status)) ?? null;
      const pkgLatestAssignment = pkgRun.reviewAssignments[0] ?? null;
      const pkgDisplayAssignment = pkgActionableAssignment ?? pkgLatestAssignment ?? null;
      const pkgNormalizedStatus = normalizedRunStatus(
        pkgRun.status,
        pkgRun.completedAt,
        pkgRun.templateSnapshot,
      );
      const pkgScore = pickOverallScore(pkgRun.templateSnapshot);
      const pkgAnswersCount =
        summarizeAnswers(pkgRun.answers) ||
        summarizeAnswers(
          isPlainObject(pkgRun.templateSnapshot)
            ? pkgRun.templateSnapshot["answers"]
            : null,
        );
      const pkgOutcome =
        packageOutcomesForTimeline.find((o) => o.assessmentRunId === pkgRun.id) ?? null;

      return {
        id: pkgRun.id,
        title: safeStr(pkgRun.title) || safeStr(pkgRun.template?.name) || `Assessment Run #${pkgRun.id}`,
        templateName: safeStr(pkgRun.template?.name) || "Assessment",
        standard: safeStr(pkgRun.template?.standard),
        version: safeStr(pkgRun.template?.version),
        category: safeStr(pkgRun.template?.category),
        status: pkgNormalizedStatus,
        dueAt: pkgRun.dueAt,
        updatedAt: pkgRun.updatedAt,
        answersCount: pkgAnswersCount,
        score: pkgScore,
        displayAssignmentStatus: safeStr(pkgDisplayAssignment?.status),
        displayAssignmentType: safeStr(pkgDisplayAssignment?.assignmentType),
        priority: safeStr(pkgDisplayAssignment?.priority),
        outcomeReleaseState: shouldHideTruvernContents ? "" : safeStr(pkgOutcome?.releaseState),
        outcomeDecision: shouldHideTruvernContents
          ? "PENDING"
          : resolveOutcomeDecision({
              decision: pkgOutcome?.decision,
              outcome: pkgOutcome?.outcome,
              meta: pkgOutcome?.meta,
              findings: pkgOutcome?.findings,
            }) || "PENDING",
        outcomeRiskLevel: shouldHideTruvernContents
          ? "—"
          : resolveOutcomeRisk({
              riskLevel: pkgOutcome?.riskLevel,
              meta: pkgOutcome?.meta,
              findings: pkgOutcome?.findings,
              templateSnapshot: pkgRun.templateSnapshot,
            }) || riskLabelFromScore(pkgScore),
        outcomeSummary: shouldHideTruvernContents
          ? ""
          : safeStr(pkgOutcome?.executiveSummary) ||
            safeStr(pkgOutcome?.summary) ||
            pickMetaString(pkgOutcome?.meta, "executiveSummary") ||
            pickFindingsString(pkgOutcome?.findings, "executiveSummary") ||
            pickFindingsString(pkgOutcome?.findings, "boardSummary"),
        hasOutcome: shouldHideTruvernContents ? false : !!pkgOutcome?.id,
        isCurrent: pkgRun.id === requestedRun.id,
        isPrimary: pkgRun.id === primaryRun.id,
      };
    })
    .sort((a, b) => {
      if (a.isPrimary && !b.isPrimary) return -1;
      if (!a.isPrimary && b.isPrimary) return 1;
      if (a.isCurrent && !b.isCurrent) return -1;
      if (!a.isCurrent && b.isCurrent) return 1;
      const aTs = a.updatedAt?.getTime() ?? 0;
      const bTs = b.updatedAt?.getTime() ?? 0;
      if (aTs !== bTs) return bTs - aTs;
      return b.id - a.id;
    });

  const packageAnswersCount = packageSummaries.reduce((sum, item) => sum + item.answersCount, 0);
  const packageLatestActivity = latestTs(
    ...packageRuns.map((r) => r.updatedAt),
    ...packageTimeline.map((evt) => evt.createdAt),
    ...(shouldHideTruvernContents
      ? []
      : packageOutcomesForTimeline.map((o) => o.updatedAt)),
  );
  const packageFirstSubmittedAt = earliestTs(...packageRuns.map((r) => r.submittedAt));
  const packageDueAt = earliestTs(...packageRuns.map((r) => r.dueAt));
  const packageCount = packageRuns.length;
  const packageHasMultiple = packageCount > 1;
  const packageCompletedCount = packageSummaries.filter((r) => r.status === "COMPLETED").length;
  const packageReleasedCount = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? 0
    : packageSummaries.filter((r) => upper(r.outcomeReleaseState) === "RELEASED").length;
  const packageOutcomeCount = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? 0
    : packageSummaries.filter((r) => r.hasOutcome).length;
  const packageReviewingCount = packageSummaries.filter(
    (r) =>
      upper(r.displayAssignmentStatus) === "ASSIGNED" ||
      upper(r.displayAssignmentStatus) === "IN_REVIEW" ||
      upper(r.displayAssignmentStatus) === "COMPLETED",
  ).length;

  const packageLaneSeed =
    safeStr(visibleOutcome?.assignmentType || displayAssignment?.assignmentType) ||
    packageSummaries.find((r) => safeStr(r.displayAssignmentType))?.displayAssignmentType ||
    "";

  const packageAverageScore = avgScore(packageSummaries.map((r) => r.score));
  const packageDecisionText = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? "Truvern release gated"
    : packageDecisionSummary(packageSummaries.map((r) => r.outcomeDecision));
  const packageRiskText = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? "Truvern release gated"
