    : packageRiskSummary(packageSummaries.map((r) => r.outcomeRiskLevel));
  const packageReleaseText = shouldHideTruvernContents
    ? "Hidden until Truvern release"
    : packageReleaseSummary(packageSummaries.map((r) => r.outcomeReleaseState));
  const packageStatus = packageRunStatusLabel(
    packageSummaries.map((r) => r.status),
    packageSummaries.map((r) => r.outcomeReleaseState),
    packageSummaries.map((r) => r.displayAssignmentStatus),
  );
  const packageCurrentIndex = Math.max(
    0,
    packageSummaries.findIndex((r) => r.id === requestedRun.id),
  );

  const controlsActorRole = isTruvernWorkspace ? "" : actorRole;

  const releaseDiffItems = buildReleaseDiffItems({
    releasedExecutiveSummary:
      safeStr(latestReleasedOutcome?.executiveSummary) ||
      safeStr(latestReleasedOutcome?.summary),
    draftExecutiveSummary:
      safeStr(latestCanonicalOutcome?.executiveSummary) ||
      safeStr(latestCanonicalOutcome?.summary),
    releasedFindings:
      safeStr(latestReleasedOutcome?.findingsText) ||
      pickMetaString(latestReleasedOutcome?.meta, "findings") ||
      pickFindingsString(latestReleasedOutcome?.findings, "findings"),
    draftFindings:
      safeStr(latestCanonicalOutcome?.findingsText) ||
      pickMetaString(latestCanonicalOutcome?.meta, "findings") ||
      pickFindingsString(latestCanonicalOutcome?.findings, "findings"),
    releasedRemediation:
      safeStr(latestReleasedOutcome?.remediation) ||
      pickMetaString(latestReleasedOutcome?.meta, "remediation") ||
      pickFindingsString(latestReleasedOutcome?.findings, "remediation"),
    draftRemediation:
      safeStr(latestCanonicalOutcome?.remediation) ||
      pickMetaString(latestCanonicalOutcome?.meta, "remediation") ||
      pickFindingsString(latestCanonicalOutcome?.findings, "remediation"),
    releasedDecision: resolveOutcomeDecision({
      decision: latestReleasedOutcome?.decision,
      outcome: latestReleasedOutcome?.outcome,
      meta: latestReleasedOutcome?.meta,
      findings: latestReleasedOutcome?.findings,
    }),
    draftDecision: resolveOutcomeDecision({
      decision: latestCanonicalOutcome?.decision,
      outcome: latestCanonicalOutcome?.outcome,
      meta: latestCanonicalOutcome?.meta,
      findings: latestCanonicalOutcome?.findings,
    }),
    releasedRisk: resolveOutcomeRisk({
      riskLevel: latestReleasedOutcome?.riskLevel,
      meta: latestReleasedOutcome?.meta,
      findings: latestReleasedOutcome?.findings,
      templateSnapshot: primaryRun.templateSnapshot,
    }),
    draftRisk: resolveOutcomeRisk({
      riskLevel: latestCanonicalOutcome?.riskLevel,
      meta: latestCanonicalOutcome?.meta,
      findings: latestCanonicalOutcome?.findings,
      templateSnapshot: primaryRun.templateSnapshot,
    }),
  });

  const canShowReleasePreviewDiff =
    !shouldHideTruvernContents &&
    !!latestCanonicalOutcome?.id &&
    !!latestReleasedOutcome?.id &&
    latestReleasedOutcome.id !== latestCanonicalOutcome.id;

  const packageInfo = {
    packageCount: packageRuns.length,
    primaryRunId: primaryRun.id,
    runIds: packageRunIds,
    submittedAt: primaryRun.submittedAt ? primaryRun.submittedAt.toISOString() : null,
    vendorId: primaryRun.vendorId ?? null,
    vendorName: safeStr(primaryRun.vendor?.name) || null,
    titles: packageRuns.map(
      (r) => safeStr(r.title) || safeStr(r.template?.name) || `Assessment Run #${r.id}`,
    ),
  };

  const isCompleted = upper(customerLifecycleStatus) === "COMPLETED";
  const isReleased = upper(customerLifecycleStatus) === "RELEASED";

  const customerPreviewEnabled = !!truvernCustomerConfirmReady;
  const isCustomerReadOnly =
    isCustomerTruvernWorkspace && !truvernCustomerAlreadyConfirmed;

  const releasePreviewOpen = isCustomerTruvernWorkspace
    ? customerPreviewEnabled && boolish(resolvedSearchParams.releasePreview)
    : isCompleted && boolish(resolvedSearchParams.releasePreview);

  const releasePreviewHref = buildPath(`/review-desk/reviews/${primaryRun.id}`, {
    releasePreview: 1,
  });

  const showPriorityReleaseCard =
    (isCustomerTruvernWorkspace && customerPreviewEnabled) ||
    (!isCustomerTruvernWorkspace && isCompleted);

  return (
    <main className="min-h-screen bg-[radial-gradient(circle_at_top,rgba(34,211,238,0.10),transparent_28%),radial-gradient(circle_at_top_right,rgba(217,70,239,0.10),transparent_24%),linear-gradient(180deg,#061019_0%,#08131f_42%,#091522_100%)] text-white">
      <div className="mx-auto max-w-7xl px-4 py-6 sm:px-5 lg:px-6">
        <div className="rounded-[24px] border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-4 backdrop-blur">
          <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2 text-xs text-white/60">
            <Link href="/review-desk" className="transition hover:text-white">
              Review Desk
            </Link>
            <span>/</span>
            <span className="text-white/80">Submitted packages</span>
            <span>/</span>
            <span className="text-white/80">
              {safeStr(primaryRun.vendor?.name) || "Vendor package"}
            </span>
            <span>/</span>
            <span className="text-cyan-200">Primary run #{primaryRun.id}</span>
            <span>/</span>
            <span className="text-white/80">
              Viewing item {packageCurrentIndex + 1} of {packageCount}
            </span>
          </div>

          <div className="mt-3 flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-3">
            <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-3">
              <Link
                href="/review-desk"
                className="inline-flex h-10 items-center justify-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-4 text-sm font-medium text-white/85 transition hover:border-white/15 hover:bg-white/10"
              >
                ← Back to Review Desk
              </Link>

              <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-fuchsia-400/25 bg-fuchsia-400/10 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.24em] text-fuchsia-200">
                {workspaceLabel}
              </div>

              <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-violet-400/25 bg-violet-400/10 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-semibold text-violet-100">
                {packageReviewLabel(packageCount)}
              </div>

              <div
                className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium ${badgeClass(
                  packageStatus,
                )}`}
              >
                Package: {packageStatus}
              </div>

              <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-white/75">
                {packageReleaseText}
              </div>

              <div
                className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium ${roleClass(
                  actorRole,
                )}`}
              >
                Your role: {titleCase(actorRole || "UNKNOWN")}
              </div>

              {snapshotId ? (
                <Link
                  href={`/vendors/${primaryRun.vendorId}/snapshots/${snapshotId}`}
                  className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-emerald-400/25 bg-emerald-400/10 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-emerald-200 transition hover:bg-emerald-400/15"
                >
                  Snapshot #{snapshotId} →
                </Link>
              ) : null}
            </div>

            <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
              <div
                className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium ${badgeClass(
                  normalizedStatus,
                )}`}
              >
                Run: {normalizedStatus}
              </div>

              {displayAssignment ? (
                <div
                  className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium ${badgeClass(
                    customerLifecycleStatus,
                  )}`}
                >
                  Package review: {customerLifecycleStatus || "—"}
                </div>
              ) : null}

              {displayAssignment?.priority ? (
                <div
                  className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium ${priorityClass(
                    safeStr(displayAssignment.priority),
                  )}`}
                >
                  Priority: {safeStr(displayAssignment.priority)}
                </div>
              ) : null}

              {!shouldHideTruvernContents && (visibleOutcome?.id ?? canonicalOutcome?.id) ? (
                <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-white/70">
                  Package Outcome #{visibleOutcome?.id ?? canonicalOutcome?.id}
                </div>
              ) : null}

              <div
                className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium ${decisionClass(
                  findingsDecision || "PENDING",
                )}`}
              >
                {prettyDecisionLabel(findingsDecision || "PENDING")}
              </div>

              <div
                className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium ${riskClass(
                  findingsRiskLevel || riskLabelFromScore(packageAverageScore),
                )}`}
              >
                {prettyRiskLabel(findingsRiskLevel || riskLabelFromScore(packageAverageScore))}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

                {showPriorityReleaseCard ? (
          <div className="mt-4 rounded-[28px] border border-rose-500/30 bg-rose-500/10 p-6 shadow-[0_0_0_1px_rgba(244,63,94,0.15)]">
            <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-4">
              <div>
                <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.25em] text-rose-200/70">
                  Release Control
                </div>
                <div className="mt-2 text-xl font-semibold text-white">
                  {isCustomerTruvernWorkspace
                    ? "Confirm and release this Truvern review"
                    : "Release this review"}
                </div>
                <div className="mt-2 max-w-2xl text-sm text-rose-100/80">
                  {isCustomerTruvernWorkspace
                    ? "Truvern has published the expert outcome. Review the final preview and confirm release to make this assessment available across Board Packet, Program State, and other customer-facing governance surfaces."
                    : "This review is complete and ready for release. Review the preview, then use the lifecycle control below to release the final outcome."}
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
                <Link
                  href={releasePreviewHref}
                  className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/15 bg-white/10 px-5 py-2.5 text-sm font-semibold text-white transition hover:bg-white/20"
                >
                  Review release preview
                </Link>

                {isCustomerTruvernWorkspace ? (
                  <form
                    action={`/api/review-desk/reviews/${primaryRun.id}/confirm-release`}
                    method="POST"
                  >
                    <button
                      type="submit"
                      className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full bg-rose-500 px-6 py-2.5 text-sm font-bold text-white shadow-lg shadow-rose-500/30 transition hover:bg-rose-400"
                    >
                      Confirm Release
                    </button>
                  </form>
                ) : (
                  <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-black/20 px-4 py-2 text-sm font-medium text-white/70">
                    Use the lifecycle action panel to release
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        ) : null}

        <div className="mt-4 rounded-[28px] border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 shadow-[0_0_0_1px_rgba(255,255,255,0.03),0_24px_70px_rgba(0,0,0,0.30)] backdrop-blur">
          <div className="grid gap-5 lg:grid-cols-[1.12fr_0.88fr]">
            <div>
              <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.24em] text-cyan-200/80">
                {packageHasMultiple ? "Package review workspace" : "Assessment review"}
              </div>
              <h1 className="mt-2 text-3xl font-semibold text-white">
                {safeStr(requestedRun.title) ||
                  safeStr(requestedRun.template?.name) ||
                  `Assessment Run #${requestedRun.id}`}
              </h1>
              <p className="mt-2 max-w-3xl text-sm leading-6 text-white/70">
                {packageHasMultiple
                  ? `This workspace is anchored to canonical primary run #${primaryRun.id} and opens one submitted vendor package containing ${packageCount} linked assessments. You are currently viewing package item ${packageCurrentIndex + 1}, but lifecycle actions and canonical findings are controlled from the primary run.`
                  : safeStr(requestedRun.description) ||
                    safeStr(requestedRun.template?.description) ||
                    workspaceBody}
              </p>

              <div className="mt-4 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/75">
                  Vendor {safeStr(primaryRun.vendor?.name) || "Unknown Vendor"}
                </div>
                <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/75">
                  Package submitted {fmtDateTime(packageFirstSubmittedAt)}
                </div>
                <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/75">
                  Package lane {assignmentTypeLabel(packageLaneSeed)}
                </div>
                <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/75">
                  Primary run #{primaryRun.id}
                </div>
                <div className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs ${decisionClass(packageDecisionText)}`}>
                  {packageDecisionText}
                </div>
                <div className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs ${riskClass(packageRiskText)}`}>
                  {packageRiskText}
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="mt-4 grid gap-3 sm:grid-cols-2 xl:grid-cols-4">
                <div className="rounded-[20px] border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/45 p-3.5">
                  <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">
                    Viewing run
                  </div>
                  <div className="mt-1.5 text-lg font-semibold text-white">#{requestedRun.id}</div>
                  <div className="mt-1 text-[11px] text-white/50">
                    Item {packageCurrentIndex + 1} of {packageCount}
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="rounded-[20px] border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/45 p-3.5">
                  <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">
                    Primary run
                  </div>
                  <div className="mt-1.5 text-lg font-semibold text-white">#{primaryRun.id}</div>
                  <div className="mt-1 text-[11px] text-white/50">Canonical package anchor</div>
                </div>

                <div className="rounded-[20px] border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/45 p-3.5">
                  <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">
                    Package answers
                  </div>
                  <div className="mt-1.5 text-lg font-semibold text-white">{packageAnswersCount}</div>
                  <div className="mt-1 text-[11px] text-white/50">
                    Combined across all included runs
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="rounded-[20px] border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/45 p-3.5">
                  <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">
                    Package avg score
                  </div>
                  <div className="mt-1.5 text-lg font-semibold text-white">
                    {packageAverageScore === null ? "—" : packageAverageScore}
                  </div>
                  <div className="mt-1 text-[11px] text-white/50">
                    {packageAverageScore === null
                      ? "No stored package scoring yet"
                      : riskLabelFromScore(packageAverageScore)}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="mt-4 rounded-[24px] border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-4">
                <div className="flex flex-wrap items-start justify-between gap-3">
                  <div>
                    <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-cyan-200/75">
                      Review progression
                    </div>
                    <div className="mt-1.5 text-lg font-semibold text-white">
                      {progression.heading}
                    </div>
                    <div className="mt-1.5 max-w-3xl text-sm leading-6 text-white/68">
                      {progression.body}
                    </div>
                  </div>

                  <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                    <div className="rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/70">
                      Canonical review state: {customerLifecycleStatus || "—"}
                    </div>
                    <div className="rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/70">
                      Next allowed action:{" "}
                      {actionLabel(nextAction, packageCount, {
                        reviewStatus: customerLifecycleStatus,
                        hasReleasedBaseline,
                        isCustomerTruvern: isCustomerTruvernWorkspace,
                        customerPreviewEnabled,
                        customerConfirmed: truvernCustomerAlreadyConfirmed,
                      })}
                    </div>
                    <div className="rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/70">
                      Package release: {packageReleaseText}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="mt-4 grid grid-cols-2 gap-2 sm:grid-cols-4">
                  {[
                    { key: 1, label: "Assigned" },
                    { key: 2, label: "In review" },
                    { key: 3, label: "Completed" },
                    { key: 4, label: "Released" },
                  ].map((step) => (
                    <div
                      key={step.key}
                      className={`rounded-2xl border px-3 py-3 text-center ${progressionStepTone(
                        step.key,
                        progression.currentStep,
                      )}`}
                    >
                      <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.18em] opacity-80">
                        Step {step.key}
                      </div>
                      <div className="mt-1 text-sm font-semibold">{step.label}</div>
                    </div>
                  ))}
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="mt-4 flex flex-wrap gap-2">
                {requestedRun.template?.standard ? (
                  <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/75">
                    {safeStr(requestedRun.template.standard)}
                  </div>
                ) : null}
                {requestedRun.template?.version ? (
                  <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/75">
                    {safeStr(requestedRun.template.version)}
                  </div>
                ) : null}
                {requestedRun.template?.category ? (
                  <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/75">
                    {safeStr(requestedRun.template.category)}
                  </div>
                ) : null}
                <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/75">
                  Answers {answersCount}
                </div>
                {sealedHash ? (
                  <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/75">
                    sealedHash {sealedHash.slice(0, 10)}…
                  </div>
                ) : null}
                {sealedAt ? (
                  <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/75">
                    Sealed {fmtDateTime(sealedAt)}
                  </div>
                ) : null}
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="space-y-4">
              <div className="rounded-[24px] border border-violet-400/18 bg-violet-400/8 p-4">
                <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.22em] text-violet-200/80">
                  Package control context
                </div>
                <div className="mt-2 text-sm leading-6 text-violet-50/85">
                  {packageHasMultiple
                    ? `You are inside a grouped submission workspace. Lifecycle actions, canonical findings, and package status are anchored to primary run #${primaryRun.id}. You may inspect any linked run below, but package progression is controlled from the primary canonical review unit.`
                    : "This submission contains one assessment run, so package view and run view are effectively the same."}
                </div>
                <div className="mt-3 flex flex-wrap gap-2 text-xs">
                  <div className="rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-black/20 px-3 py-1 text-white/75">
                    {shouldHideTruvernContents
                      ? "Outcomes hidden until Truvern release"
                      : `Outcomes saved ${packageOutcomeCount}/${packageCount}`}
                  </div>
                  <div className="rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-black/20 px-3 py-1 text-white/75">
                    {shouldHideTruvernContents
                      ? "Released baseline pending"
                      : `Released ${packageReleasedCount}/${packageCount}`}
                  </div>
                  <div className="rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-black/20 px-3 py-1 text-white/75">
                    Active review entries {packageReviewingCount}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>

              {isCustomerReadOnly ? (
                <div className="rounded-[24px] border border-amber-400/18 bg-amber-400/8 p-4">
                  <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-amber-100">
                    Customer workspace is read-only for Truvern review
                  </div>
                  <div className="mt-2 text-sm leading-6 text-amber-50/85">
                    This package is assigned to Truvern. Your organization can monitor status,
                    vendor context, and lifecycle progress here, but findings, decisions, and release actions remain locked until Truvern publishes and you confirm the expert release.
                  </div>
                </div>
              ) : null}

              <ReviewActionPanel
                runId={primaryRun.id}
                assignmentId={canonicalAssignmentId}
                assignmentStatus={customerLifecycleStatus}
                assignmentType={effectiveAssignmentType}
                priority={safeStr(displayAssignment?.priority)}
                requestedBy={requestorName}
                assignedTo={assignedName}
                note={safeStr(displayAssignment?.note)}
                createdAtLabel={fmtDateTime(displayAssignment?.createdAt || primaryRun.createdAt)}
                updatedAtLabel={fmtDateTime(displayAssignment?.updatedAt || primaryRun.updatedAt)}
                hasCurrentOutcome={shouldHideTruvernContents ? false : !!(visibleOutcome?.id ?? canonicalOutcome?.id)}
                outcomeDecision={findingsDecision}
                outcomeRiskLevel={findingsRiskLevel || riskLabelFromScore(packageAverageScore)}
                outcomeReleaseState={
                  isCustomerTruvernWorkspace && !truvernCustomerAlreadyConfirmed
                    ? "INTERNAL"
                    : safeStr(visibleOutcome?.releaseState || canonicalOutcome?.releaseState)
                }
                outcomeSavedAtLabel={lastFindingsSavedAt}
                packageInfo={packageInfo}
                actorRole={controlsActorRole}
                availableCredits={availableCredits}
                reservedCredits={reservedCredits}
                consumedCredits={consumedCredits}
                minimumBalanceAlert={minimumBalanceAlert}
                hasReleasedBaseline={shouldHideTruvernContents ? false : hasReleasedBaseline}
                hasWorkingDraft={shouldHideTruvernContents ? false : !!latestWorkingOutcome?.id}
                isCustomerReadOnly={isCustomerReadOnly}
                disableLifecycleActions={isCustomerReadOnly}
              />
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="mt-4 rounded-[26px] border border-emerald-400/18 bg-[linear-gradient(180deg,rgba(10,18,27,0.96),rgba(7,14,22,0.94))] p-5 shadow-[0_0_0_1px_rgba(16,185,129,0.06),0_22px_60px_rgba(0,0,0,0.28)]">
          <div className="flex flex-wrap items-start justify-between gap-3">
            <div>
              <div className="text-[11px] font-semibold uppercase tracking-[0.24em] text-emerald-200/80">
                Canonical current outcome
              </div>
              <h2 className="mt-1.5 text-xl font-semibold text-white">Board-style summary</h2>
              <p className="mt-1.5 max-w-3xl text-sm leading-6 text-white/68">
                This panel reflects the latest customer-visible{" "}
                <span className="font-medium text-white/85">AssessmentReviewOutcome</span> for the
                package primary run and should be the source used by downstream governance surfaces.
              </p>
            </div>

            <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
              <div
                className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium ${decisionPillTone(
                  findingsDecision || "PENDING",
                )}`}
              >
                Decision: {prettyDecisionLabel(findingsDecision || "PENDING")}
              </div>
              <div
                className={`inline-flex items-center rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium ${riskPillTone(
                  findingsRiskLevel || riskLabelFromScore(packageAverageScore),
                )}`}
              >
                Residual risk: {prettyRiskLabel(findingsRiskLevel || riskLabelFromScore(packageAverageScore))}
              </div>
              <div className="inline-flex items-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs font-medium text-white/70">
                {lastFindingsSavedAt ? `Saved ${lastFindingsSavedAt}` : "No saved outcome yet"}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="mt-4 grid gap-4 lg:grid-cols-[1.15fr_0.85fr]">
            <div className="rounded-[20px] border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-4">
              <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">
                Executive summary
              </div>
              <div className="mt-2 text-sm leading-7 text-white/80">
                {findingsExecutiveSummary ||
                  (shouldHideTruvernContents
                    ? "Truvern is currently reviewing this package. Findings and recommendations will appear here after the Truvern expert release is published and confirmed."
                    : "No executive summary has been saved yet.")}
              </div>

              <div className="mt-4 grid gap-3 sm:grid-cols-2">
                <div className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-3.5">
                  <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">
                    Key findings
                  </div>
                  <div className="mt-2 text-sm leading-6 text-white/75">
                    {findingsText ||
                      (shouldHideTruvernContents
                        ? "Working Truvern findings remain hidden until the expert release is published and confirmed."
                        : "No structured findings have been saved yet.")}
                  </div>
                </div>

                <div className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-3.5">
                  <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">
                    Remediation / follow-up
                  </div>
                  <div className="mt-2 text-sm leading-6 text-white/75">
                    {findingsRemediation ||
                      (shouldHideTruvernContents
                        ? "Remediation guidance will appear after Truvern publishes and the customer confirms release."
                        : "No remediation guidance has been saved yet.")}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="space-y-3">
              <div className="rounded-[20px] border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-4">
                <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">
                  Reviewer note
                </div>
                <div className="mt-2 text-sm leading-6 text-white/75">
                  {findingsReviewerNote ||
                    (shouldHideTruvernContents
                      ? "Reviewer notes are hidden until the Truvern release is available and confirmed."
                      : "No reviewer note has been saved yet.")}
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="rounded-[20px] border border-cyan-400/18 bg-cyan-400/8 p-4">
                <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-cyan-100">{snapshotTitle}</div>
                <div className="mt-2.5 space-y-1.5 text-sm text-cyan-100/78">
                  <div>
                    <span className="font-medium text-cyan-50">Decision:</span>{" "}
                    {prettyDecisionLabel(findingsDecision || "PENDING")}
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <span className="font-medium text-cyan-50">Residual risk:</span>{" "}
                    {prettyRiskLabel(findingsRiskLevel || riskLabelFromScore(packageAverageScore))}
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <span className="font-medium text-cyan-50">Review lane:</span> {laneLabel}
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <span className="font-medium text-cyan-50">Primary run:</span> #{primaryRun.id}
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <span className="font-medium text-cyan-50">Viewed run:</span> #{requestedRun.id}
                  </div>
                  <div>
                    <span className="font-medium text-cyan-50">Assignment:</span>{" "}
                    {safeStr(displayAssignment?.status) || "—"}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div className="mt-4">
          <ReviewFindingsPanel
            runId={primaryRun.id}
            assignmentId={canonicalAssignmentId}
            initialExecutiveSummary={findingsExecutiveSummary}
            initialDecision={findingsDecision}
            initialRiskLevel={findingsRiskLevel || riskLabelFromScore(packageAverageScore)}
            initialFindings={findingsText}
            initialRemediation={findingsRemediation}
            initialReviewerNote={findingsReviewerNote}
            lastSavedAtLabel={lastFindingsSavedAt}
            outcomeId={shouldHideTruvernContents ? null : visibleOutcome?.id ?? canonicalOutcome?.id ?? null}
            assignmentType={effectiveAssignmentType}
            assignmentStatus={customerLifecycleStatus}
            releaseState={
              shouldHideTruvernContents
                ? ""
                : safeStr(visibleOutcome?.releaseState || canonicalOutcome?.releaseState)
            }
            packageInfo={packageInfo}
            actorRole={controlsActorRole}
            previousReleasedExecutiveSummary={
              shouldHideTruvernContents
                ? ""
                : safeStr(latestReleasedOutcome?.executiveSummary) ||
                  safeStr(latestReleasedOutcome?.summary)
            }
            previousReleasedDecision={
              shouldHideTruvernContents
                ? ""
                : resolveOutcomeDecision({
                    decision: latestReleasedOutcome?.decision,
                    outcome: latestReleasedOutcome?.outcome,
                    meta: latestReleasedOutcome?.meta,
                    findings: latestReleasedOutcome?.findings,
                  })
            }
            previousReleasedRiskLevel={
              shouldHideTruvernContents
                ? ""
                : resolveOutcomeRisk({
                    riskLevel: latestReleasedOutcome?.riskLevel,
                    meta: latestReleasedOutcome?.meta,
                    findings: latestReleasedOutcome?.findings,
                    templateSnapshot: primaryRun.templateSnapshot,
                  })
            }
            previousReleasedFindings={
              shouldHideTruvernContents
                ? ""
                : safeStr(latestReleasedOutcome?.findingsText) ||
                  pickMetaString(latestReleasedOutcome?.meta, "findings") ||
                  pickFindingsString(latestReleasedOutcome?.findings, "findings")
            }
            previousReleasedRemediation={
              shouldHideTruvernContents
                ? ""
                : safeStr(latestReleasedOutcome?.remediation) ||
                  pickMetaString(latestReleasedOutcome?.meta, "remediation") ||
                  pickFindingsString(latestReleasedOutcome?.findings, "remediation")
            }
            previousReleasedReviewerNote={
              shouldHideTruvernContents
                ? ""
                : safeStr(latestReleasedOutcome?.reviewerNote) ||
                  safeStr(latestReleasedOutcome?.note) ||
                  pickMetaString(latestReleasedOutcome?.meta, "reviewerNote") ||
                  pickFindingsString(latestReleasedOutcome?.findings, "reviewerNote")
            }
            isCustomerReadOnly={isCustomerReadOnly}
          />
        </div>

        <div className="mt-4 grid gap-4 lg:grid-cols-[0.95fr_1.05fr]">
          <section className="rounded-[24px] border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 shadow-[0_0_0_1px_rgba(255,255,255,0.03),0_20px_60px_rgba(0,0,0,0.26)] backdrop-blur">
            <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
              <div>
                <div className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">Vendor context</div>
                <div className="mt-1 text-sm text-white/55">
                  Business, contact, and scoring details tied to this review package.
                </div>
              </div>
              {primaryRun.vendor?.id ? (
                <Link
                  href={`/vendors/${primaryRun.vendor.id}`}
                  className="inline-flex h-9 items-center justify-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-4 text-sm font-medium text-white/80 transition hover:bg-white/10"
                >
                  Open vendor →
                </Link>
              ) : null}
            </div>

            <div className="mt-4 grid gap-3 sm:grid-cols-2">
              <div className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-3.5">
                <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">Vendor name</div>
                <div className="mt-1.5 text-sm font-medium text-white">
                  {safeStr(primaryRun.vendor?.name) || "—"}
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-3.5">
                <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">Contact</div>
                <div className="mt-1.5 text-sm font-medium text-white">
                  {safeStr(primaryRun.vendor?.contactName) ||
                    safeStr(primaryRun.vendor?.contactEmail) ||
                    "—"}
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-3.5">
                <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">Criticality</div>
                <div className="mt-1.5 text-sm font-medium text-white">
                  {safeStr(primaryRun.vendor?.criticality) || "—"}
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-3.5">
                <div className="text-[11px] uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/45">Materiality</div>
                <div className="mt-1.5 text-sm font-medium text-white">
                  {safeStr(primaryRun.vendor?.materiality) || "—"}
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </section>

          <section className="rounded-[24px] border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 shadow-[0_0_0_1px_rgba(255,255,255,0.03),0_20px_60px_rgba(0,0,0,0.26)] backdrop-blur">
            <div className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">Package timeline</div>
            <div className="mt-1 text-sm text-white/55">
              Lifecycle and canonical outcome activity for the primary package.
            </div>

            <div className="mt-4 space-y-3">
              {(shouldHideTruvernContents
                ? primaryTimeline.filter((evt) => upper(evt.action) !== "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_FINDINGS_SAVED")
                : primaryTimeline
              ).length ? (
                (shouldHideTruvernContents
                  ? primaryTimeline.filter((evt) => upper(evt.action) !== "ASSESSMENT_REVIEW_FINDINGS_SAVED")
                  : primaryTimeline
                ).map((evt) => (
                  <div
                    key={evt.id}
                    className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/35 p-3.5"
                  >
                    <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center justify-between gap-3">
                      <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-white">
                        {normalizeTimelineAction(evt.action)}
                      </div>
                      <div className="text-xs text-white/50">{fmtDateTime(evt.createdAt)}</div>
                    </div>
                    <div className="mt-1.5 text-sm text-white/70">
                      {safeStr(evt.summary) || "No summary provided."}
                    </div>
                  </div>
                ))
              ) : (
                <div className="rounded-2xl border border-dashed border-white/10 bg-slate-950/20 p-4 text-sm text-white/50">
                  No timeline activity available yet.
                </div>
              )}
            </div>
          </section>
        </div>

        <section className="mt-4 rounded-[24px] border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 shadow-[0_0_0_1px_rgba(255,255,255,0.03),0_20px_60px_rgba(0,0,0,0.26)] backdrop-blur">
          <div className="flex flex-wrap items-start justify-between gap-3">
            <div>
              <div className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">Submitted package</div>
              <div className="mt-1 text-sm text-white/55">
                Per-run status, scoring, and saved outcome coverage across this package.
              </div>
            </div>

            <div className="flex flex-wrap gap-2">
              <div className="rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/75">
                Latest activity {fmtDateTime(packageLatestActivity)}
              </div>
              <div className="rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-white/5 px-3 py-1 text-xs text-white/75">
                Earliest due {fmtDate(packageDueAt)}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div className="mt-4 grid gap-3">
            {packageSummaries.map((item) => (
              <div
                key={item.id}
                className={`rounded-[18px] border p-4 ${
                  item.isPrimary
                    ? "border-violet-400/22 bg-violet-400/8"
                    : item.isCurrent
                      ? "border-cyan-400/22 bg-cyan-400/8"
                      : "border-white/10 bg-white/5"
                }`}
              >
                <div className="flex flex-col gap-3 xl:flex-row xl:items-start xl:justify-between">
                  <div className="min-w-0">
                    <div className="flex flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                      <div className="truncate text-sm font-semibold text-white">{item.title}</div>
                      {item.isPrimary ? (
                        <span className="rounded-full border border-violet-400/30 bg-violet-400/12 px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium text-violet-200">
                          Primary package run
                        </span>
                      ) : null}
                      {!item.isPrimary && item.isCurrent ? (
                        <span className="rounded-full border border-cyan-400/30 bg-cyan-400/12 px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium text-cyan-200">
                          Current view
                        </span>
                      ) : null}
                      <span
                        className={`rounded-full border px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium ${badgeClass(
                          item.status,
                        )}`}
                      >
                        {item.status}
                      </span>
                      {item.displayAssignmentStatus ? (
                        <span
                          className={`rounded-full border px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium ${badgeClass(
                            item.displayAssignmentStatus,
                          )}`}
                        >
                          Review {item.displayAssignmentStatus}
                        </span>
                      ) : null}
                      {item.priority ? (
                        <span
                          className={`rounded-full border px-2.5 py-1 text-[11px] font-medium ${priorityClass(
                            item.priority,
                          )}`}
                        >
                          {item.priority}
                        </span>
                      ) : null}
                    </div>

                    <div className="mt-2 text-xs text-white/55">
                      {[item.templateName, item.standard, item.version, item.category]
                        .filter(Boolean)
                        .join(" · ") || "Assessment"}
                    </div>

                    <div className="mt-3 flex flex-wrap gap-2 text-[11px] text-white/55">
                      <span className="rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-black/20 px-2.5 py-1">
                        Run #{item.id}
                      </span>
                      <span className="rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-black/20 px-2.5 py-1">
                        Answers {item.answersCount}
                      </span>
                      <span className="rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-black/20 px-2.5 py-1">
                        Due {fmtDate(item.dueAt)}
                      </span>
                      {item.score !== null ? (
                        <span className={`rounded-full border px-2.5 py-1 ${badgeClass(String(item.score >= 80 ? "COMPLETED" : item.score >= 50 ? "PENDING" : "RELEASED"))}`}>
                          Score {item.score}
                        </span>
                      ) : null}
                      {item.outcomeReleaseState ? (
                        <span
                          className={`rounded-full border px-2.5 py-1 ${releaseStateClass(
                            item.outcomeReleaseState,
                          )}`}
                        >
                          Release {item.outcomeReleaseState}
                        </span>
                      ) : null}
                    </div>

                    {item.outcomeSummary ? (
                      <div className="mt-3 rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-black/20 p-3 text-sm leading-6 text-white/72">
                        {item.outcomeSummary}
                      </div>
                    ) : (
                      <div className="mt-3 rounded-2xl border border-dashed border-white/10 bg-black/10 p-3 text-sm leading-6 text-white/50">
                        {shouldHideTruvernContents
                          ? "Outcome content is hidden until Truvern publishes the expert release and the customer confirms it."
                          : "No saved findings summary for this run yet."}
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>

                  <div className="flex shrink-0 flex-wrap items-center gap-2">
                    {item.isPrimary ? (
                      <div className="inline-flex h-10 items-center justify-center rounded-full border border-violet-400/25 bg-violet-400/10 px-4 text-sm font-medium text-violet-200">
                        Canonical workspace
                      </div>
                    ) : (
                      <div className="inline-flex h-10 items-center justify-center rounded-full border border-white/10 bg-black/20 px-4 text-sm font-medium text-white/45">
                        Package member
                      </div>
                    )}
                  </div>
                </div>
              </div>
            ))}
          </div>
        </section>

        {releasePreviewOpen ? (
          <div className="fixed inset-0 z-50 flex">
            <Link
              href={`/review-desk/reviews/${primaryRun.id}`}
              className="flex-1 bg-black/70 backdrop-blur-sm"
            />
            <div className="h-full w-full max-w-3xl overflow-y-auto border-l border-white/10 bg-[#070b17] shadow-[-20px_0_60px_rgba(0,0,0,0.5)]">
              <div className="sticky top-0 border-b border-white/10 bg-[#070b17]/95 px-6 py-4 backdrop-blur">
                <div className="flex items-center justify-between">
                  <div>
                    <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.2em] text-white/50">
                      Release Preview
                    </div>
                    <div className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">
                      Customer-visible changes
                    </div>
                  </div>
                  <Link
                    href={`/review-desk/reviews/${primaryRun.id}`}
                    className="text-sm text-white/70 hover:text-white"
                  >
                    Close
                  </Link>
                </div>
              </div>

              <div className="p-6 space-y-6">
                <div className="text-sm text-white/60">
                  This preview shows what will become visible after release.
                </div>

                {canShowReleasePreviewDiff ? (
                  <div className="space-y-4">
                    {releaseDiffItems.map((item) => (
                      <div key={item.label} className="rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-white/[0.03] p-4">
                        <div className="flex items-center justify-between gap-3">
                          <div className="text-sm font-semibold text-white">{item.label}</div>
                          <div className={`rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs ${item.changed ? "border-amber-400/30 bg-amber-400/12 text-amber-100" : "border-white/10 bg-white/5 text-white/60"}`}>
                            {item.changed ? "Changed" : "Unchanged"}
                          </div>
                        </div>

                        <div className="mt-3 grid gap-3 md:grid-cols-2">
                          <div className="rounded-xl border border-white/10 p-3">
                            <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-white/40">
                              Released
                            </div>
                            <div className="mt-2">
                              {upper(item.label) === "DECISION" || upper(item.label) === "RESIDUAL RISK" ? (
                                <span className={`inline-flex rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs ${diffPillTone(item.label, item.released)}`}>
                                  {diffDisplayValue(item.label, item.released)}
                                </span>
                              ) : (
                                <div className="whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm text-white/80">
                                  {item.released}
                                </div>
                              )}
                            </div>
                          </div>

                          <div className="rounded-xl border border-white/10 p-3">
                            <div className="text-xs uppercase tracking-[0.18em] text-white/40">
                              Draft
                            </div>
                            <div className="mt-2">
                              {upper(item.label) === "DECISION" || upper(item.label) === "RESIDUAL RISK" ? (
                                <span className={`inline-flex rounded-full border px-3 py-1 text-xs ${diffPillTone(item.label, item.draft)}`}>
                                  {diffDisplayValue(item.label, item.draft)}
                                </span>
                              ) : (
                                <div className="whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm text-white/80">
                                  {item.draft}
                                </div>
                              )}
                            </div>
                          </div>
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    ))}
                  </div>
                ) : (
                  <div className="space-y-4">
                    <div className="rounded-xl border border-white/10 p-4">
                      <div className="text-xs text-white/50">Executive Summary</div>
                      <div className="mt-2 whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm text-white">
                        {findingsExecutiveSummary || "—"}
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    <div className="grid grid-cols-2 gap-4">
                      <div className="rounded-xl border border-white/10 p-4">
                        <div className="text-xs text-white/50">Decision</div>
                        <div className="mt-2 text-sm text-white">
                          {prettyDecisionLabel(findingsDecision)}
                        </div>
                      </div>

                      <div className="rounded-xl border border-white/10 p-4">
                        <div className="text-xs text-white/50">Residual Risk</div>
                        <div className="mt-2 text-sm text-white">
                          {prettyRiskLabel(findingsRiskLevel)}
                        </div>
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    <div className="rounded-xl border border-white/10 p-4">
                      <div className="text-xs text-white/50">Findings</div>
                      <div className="mt-2 whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm text-white">
                        {findingsText || "—"}
                      </div>
                    </div>

                    <div className="rounded-xl border border-white/10 p-4">
                      <div className="text-xs text-white/50">Remediation</div>
                      <div className="mt-2 whitespace-pre-wrap text-sm text-white">
                        {findingsRemediation || "—"}
                      </div>
                    </div>
                  </div>
                )}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        ) : null}

        <section className="mt-4 rounded-[24px] border border-white/10 bg-white/5 p-5 shadow-[0_0_0_1px_rgba(255,255,255,0.03),0_20px_60px_rgba(0,0,0,0.26)] backdrop-blur">
          <div className="text-lg font-semibold text-white">Answer payload preview</div>
          <div className="mt-1 text-sm text-white/55">
            Combined package answer payload for troubleshooting and release verification.
          </div>
          <pre className="mt-4 overflow-x-auto rounded-2xl border border-white/10 bg-slate-950/40 p-4 text-xs leading-6 text-white/75">
            {renderJsonPreview(
              packageRuns.map((pkgRun) => ({
                runId: pkgRun.id,
                title:
                  safeStr(pkgRun.title) ||
                  safeStr(pkgRun.template?.name) ||
                  `Assessment Run #${pkgRun.id}`,
                answers: pkgRun.answers ?? null,
              })),
            )}
          </pre>
        </section>
      </div>
    </main>
  );
}

// lib/truvern-ops-access.ts
import { auth } from "@clerk/nextjs/server";

function safeStr(v: unknown) {
  return typeof v === "string" ? v.trim() : "";
}

export function parseAllowedUsers() {
  return safeStr(process.env.TRUVERN_OPS_USERS)
    .split(",")
    .map((x) => x.trim())
    .filter(Boolean);
}

export async function requireTruvernOperator() {
  const { userId } = await auth();

  if (!userId) {
    throw new Error("Unauthorized");
  }

  const allowed = parseAllowedUsers();

  if (!allowed.includes(userId)) {
    throw new Error("Not authorized for Truvern ops.");
  }

  return { userId };
}

export async function isTruvernOperator() {
  try {
    const { userId } = await auth();

    if (!userId) return false;

    const allowed = parseAllowedUsers();
    return allowed.includes(userId);
  } catch {
    return false;
  }
}

// middleware.ts
import { clerkMiddleware, createRouteMatcher } from "@clerk/nextjs/server";
import { NextResponse } from "next/server";

/**
 * Public routes (no auth required)
 */
const isPublicRoute = createRouteMatcher([
  "/",
  "/pricing(.*)",
  "/contact(.*)",
  "/features(.*)",
  "/trust-network(.*)",
  "/assessment/demo(.*)",
  "/sign-in(.*)",
  "/sign-up(.*)",
  "/sso-callback(.*)",

  // Public / tokenized / external flows
  "/board-packet(.*)",
  "/vendor-assessment(.*)",
  "/api/vendor-assessment/(.*)",
  "/api/public/(.*)",

  // Webhooks / callbacks
  "/api/webhooks/(.*)",
  "/api/stripe/(.*)",

  // Keep reachable, but do not force users through it
  "/select-org(.*)",
]);

/**
 * API routes that must NOT redirect to /sign-in from middleware.
 * Route handlers should return JSON/CSV status codes themselves.
 */
const isApiNoRedirectRoute = createRouteMatcher([
  "/api/issues(.*)",

  // Canonical trust network export route
  "/api/trust-network-export(.*)",

  // Legacy shim route must also not redirect
  "/api/trust-network/export(.*)",

  "/api/auth/(.*)",
]);

export default clerkMiddleware(async (authFn, req) => {
  const res = NextResponse.next();

  // Always hydrate Clerk request auth
  const a = await authFn();

  if (process.env.NODE_ENV !== "production") {
    res.headers.set("x-truvern-mw", "1");
  }

  // Public routes always allowed
  if (isPublicRoute(req)) return res;

  // API routes: never redirect from middleware
  if (isApiNoRedirectRoute(req)) return res;

  // Protected routes: sign-in required only
  if (!a.userId) {
    return a.redirectToSignIn({ returnBackUrl: req.url });
  }

  /**
   * IMPORTANT:
   * Do NOT perform organization gating in middleware.
   * Let server pages/routes resolve org context via requireDbOrganization().
   * This prevents select-org/onboarding loops and keeps org switching invisible.
   */

  return res;
});

export const config = {
  matcher: [
    "/((?!_next|[^?]*\\.(?:html?|css|js(?!on)|jpe?g|webp|png|gif|svg|ttf|woff2?|ico|csv|docx?|xlsx?|zip|webmanifest)).*)",
    "/(api|trpc)(.*)",
  ],
};
